 	 28 “Lekeni imunu ayo koka, kuya ketingana ne imtumwa miyaghe iyang'ali yomdahi sendi chidogho. Kamghogha kamkinda halumelo. Kalonga, ‘Unilihe sendi tsangu!’ 29 Imtumwa miyaghe kamtowela ghamaghoti, kamlomba, ‘Unidudumile, nitsokuliha.’ 30 Lekeni yeye kalema, kaghenda kumwika miyaghe mchifungo, mbaka hayatsoliha deni lila. 31 Iwatumwa wangi hawonile achila ichilawile, wasing'inika sideke, waghenda kumlongela imndewa chila chinu ichilawile. 32 Kuya imndewa kamkema mng'anda imtumwa ayo, kamlongela, ‘Ghweghwe imtumwa wihile. Nikuleghusila deni lyose kwaapfila tsakunilomba nitende apfo. 33 Tsakubamighwa umwonele libatsi imtumwa miyagho ka nene pfanikwonele libatsi.’ 34 Apfo imndewa ayo kona maya sideke, kamwika mchifungo yadununzighwe mbaka hayatsoliha deni lyose.”
 	 35 Kuya Yesu kaghendelela kulonga, “Apfi pfifo Aba wangu iyali kulanga pfayatsowatendelani mng'aleka kuwaleghusila wandughu tsenu ghamatotso ghawo kulawa mne mimoyo yenu.”
 
 Matei 19

 Ukwileka

 (Maliki 10:1-12)

 	1 Yesu hayamalitse kulonga mbuli atso, kalawa isi ya Galilaya kaghenda mne isi ya Yudeya, kumwambu kwe ghumto Yoridani. 2 Iwanu wengi wamuwinza, naye kawahonetsa.
 	 3 Mafarisayo wangi wamghendela Yesu wamghetse. Wamghutsa, “Angu pfinogha immale kumleka mwehe wake kwa totso lyolyose?” 4 Yesu kawedika, “Ng'amsomile bae mne Ghamaandiko Mahenzeluka, ka kulawa mwanduso Imulungu tsakalumba immale ne ipinga? 5 Apfo Imulungu kalonga, ‘Kwa ichinu chino, mmale katsomleka aba wake na mai wake, katselunga na mwehe wake, nawo weli watsokuwa lukuli lumwe?’ 6 Apfo si weli keli, ila lukuli lumwe. Apfo chayalungile Imulungu, imunu yaleke kuchibaghula.”
 	 7 Mafarisayo wamghutsa, “Ebali lelo Musa tsakalaghitsa immale yamwing'e mwehe wake talaka na kumleka?”
 	 8 Yesu kawedika, “Musa tsakawalekelela muwaleke wehe tsenu kwaapfila imimoyo yenu mikomu. Lekeni ng'aiwile pfino bae kulawa mwanduso. 9 Nowalongelani, imunu wowose iyomleka mwehe wake, ila kwa ughoni, na ukukwela ipinga yungi, ayo kotenda ughoni.”
 	 10 Iwanang'ina wake wamlongela, “Ka apfo pfipfo pfaili kwe immale na mwehe wake. Ng'apfu kuleka ukukwelela.”
 	 11 Yesu kawedika, “Si chila imunu bae iyodaha kuitoghola mbuli ino, ila awala iweng'ighwe ne Imulungu. 12 Kuna ipfinu pfingi ipfiwatenda iwamale waleke kukwela, kwaapfila wamwenga welekighwa pfipfo, na wamwenga watendighwa apfo ne iwanu. Wamwenga ng'awokwela bae kwaajili ye undewa wa kulanga. Imunu iyodaha kuitoghola imbuli ino, leka yaitoghole.”
 	
 Yesu kowabaliki iwana wadowado

 (Maliki 10:13-16; Luka 18:15-17)

 	13 Kuya iwanu wangi wamghalila Yesu iwana wadowado awekile ghamoko na kuwalombela, lekeni iwanang'ina wake wawakembela iwanu awo iwawaghalile iwana. 14 Yesu kalonga, “Muwaleke iwana wadowado watse kuna nene, mleke kuwaghoma kwaapfila undewa wa kulanga wa iwanu iwali ka iwana wano.” 15 Kawekila ghamoko, kuya koka hanu aho.
 	
 Imbwanga tajiri

 (Maliki 10:17-31; Luka 18:18-30)

 	16 Imunu yumwe kamghendela Yesu kamghutsa, “Mlangulitsi, angu nende choni chinoghile ili niubokele ughima wa ghamatsuwa ghose?” 17 Yesu kamwidika, “Ebali kwonighutsa imbuli ye ichinu chinoghile? Hana yumwe yaliyeka iyanoghile. Ung'abama kwingila mne ughima wa ghamatsuwa ghose, ughakinde ghamalaghitso ghe Imulungu.”
 	 18 Imunu yula kamghutsa, “Ghamalaghitso ghachi?” Yesu kamwidika, “Aghano, uleke kukoma, uleke ughoni, uleke ubapfi na uleke kulonga ughutsu, 19 uwategheletse aba wako na mai wako, umnoghele miyagho ka pfawinoghela ghumwenyegho.”
 	 20 Imsongolo yula kamlongela, “Agha ghose nighakinda. Lelo nitende choni keli?” 21 Yesu kamwidika, “Ung'abama kuwa imunu yatimilike, ughende ukautse ipfinu pfako pfose, uweng'e tsisendi iwahingwa, naghwe kutsakuwa na hatsina kulanga. Kuya utse uniwinze.” 22 Imsongolo yula hayahulike apfo, koka kwa usungu, kwaapfila tsakana mali nyingi.
 	 23 Kuya Yesu kawalongela iwanang'ina wake, “Nowalongela ghendo, itsakuwa pfikomu kwa tajiri kwingila mne undewa wa kulanga. 24 Kuya nowalongelani, pfibewe kwe ingamiya kwingila mchonzo mwe sindano, kubita tajiri kwingila mne undewa we Imulungu.”
 	 25 Iwanang'ina wake hawahulike apfo, wakangawala ghendo, wamghutsa, “Lelo yuhi iyodaha kukombolighwa?” 26 Yesu kawalola kuya kawalongela, “Kwe imunu chinu chino ng'achidahika bae, lekeni kwe Imulungu ghose ghodahika.”
 	 27 Petiri kamwidika, “Tuleka chila chinu twokuwinza ghweghwe. Lelo tutsopata choni?” 28 Yesu kawalongela, “Nowalongelani ghendo, mne isi iikutsa, Imwana we Imunu hayatsokala hane chighoda chake cha utunitso, mwemwe imniwinzile nene pfipfila mtsokala mne pfighoda kumi na pfili, kughahigha makabila kumi na meli gha Isiraeli. 29 Na imunu wowose iyalekile tsing'anda, au kaka tsake, au lumbu tsake, au aba wake, au mai wake, au iwanaghe, au imighunda yake kwaajili yangu, ayo katsobokela mala kumi, na katsohala ughima wa ghamatsuwa ghose. 30 Lekeni awala wa mwanduso watsakuwa wa utsighilo, na wautsighilo watsakuwa wamwanduso.
 
 Matei 20

 Iwosang'ana mne mghunda ghwa mitsabibu

 	1 “Undewa we Imulungu weghala ne imunu yane mghunda, iyalawile lupfilipfili kaghenda kubama iwanu wakasang'ane mne mghunda ghwake. 2 Katoghola kuwaliha sendi tsa litsuwa limwe, kuya kawaghala mne mghunda ghwake. 3 Masaa madatu hambele koka keli, kawona iwanu wangi wema mne ghulilo wahela sang'ano. 4 Kawalongela, ‘Mwemwe mwose mghende mne mghunda ghwangu mkasang'ane, nitsowaliha pfinoghile.’ 5 Nawo waghenda. Kuya kaghenda keli saa sita na saa tisa, katenda pfipfila. 6 Haipfikile saa kumi na imwe koka keli, kawona iwanu wangi wema hane ghulilo, kawaghutsa, ‘Ebali mwimile hano misi yose bila sang'ano?’ 7 Iwanu awo wamwidika, ‘Kwaapfila haduhu imunu iyatwing'ile sang'ano.’ Kawalongela, ‘Namwe pfipfila mghende mkasang'ane mne mghunda ghwangu.’
 	 8 “Nemihe haipfikile, imunu yane mghunda kamlongela mwimilitsi wake, ‘Uwakeme iwanu iwasang'ane, uwalihe sendi tsawo, wanduse na wautsighilo kuya awala iwalongole.’ 9 Iwanu iwasang'ane kwandusila saa kumi na imwe hawatsile, chila munu kabokela malilho gha litsuwa limwe. 10 Apfo awala iwalongole kusang'ana hawatsile, tsawalolela kubokela sendi nyingi, lekeni chila munu kabokela dinali imwe. 11 Hawabokele maliho ghawo, wandusa kumsing'inikila ayula yane mghunda. 12 Walonga, ‘Iwanu wano iwatsile kusang'ana nemihe, wasang'ana kwa saa limwe liliheka, lekeni kuwaliha ka pfautulihe twetwe itusang'ane misi yose mlutsua.’
 	 13 “Naye kamwidika yumwe wawo, ‘Sale yangu, sikubunzile bae. Apfi ghweghwe ng'utoghole kusang'ana kwa malilho gha litsuwa limwe? 14 Lelo usole ichili chako uke. Nene nobama kumwing'a ayula wa utsighilo ka pfanikwing'ile ghweghwe. 15 Angu ng'apfinoghile bae nene kutenda achila chanibama kwa sendi tsangu mwenyegho? Au kwakona chepfu kwaapfila nene namluso?’ ”
 	 16 Kuya Yesu kamalitsa kwa ukulonga, “Apfo, wa utsighilo katsakuwa wa mwanduso, na ayula wamwanduso katsakuwa wautsighilo.”
 	
 Yesu kolonga lwakadatu imbuli ya lifwa lyake

 (Maliki 10:32-34; Luka 18:31-34)

 	17 Yesu hayang'ali yoghenda Yerusalemu kawasola iwanang'ina kumi na weli waliyeka, kawalongela, 18 “Mlole, twogheluka Yerusalemu, ako Imwana we Imunu katsakwing'ighwa mne ghamoko ghe iwatambika wakulu ne iwalangulitsi we ghamalaghitso. Nawo watsomhigha yakomighwe. 19 Kuya watsomghala kwe iwanu iwali si Wayahudi, nawo watsombetsa, watsomtsipula na watsomkoma kwa kumuwamba mna msalaba, lekeni ghamatsuwa madatu hambele katsotsilihuka!”
 	
 Mai wawo Jakobu na Yohane kowalombela ukulu iwanaghe

 (Maliki 10:35-45)

 	20 Kuya mai we iwana wa Sebedayo kamghendela Yesu hamwe ne iwanaghe, katowa ghamaghoti, kamlomba amtendele choyobama.
 	 21 Yesu kamghutsa, “Ubama choni.”
 	Ipinga ayo kamwidika, “Chondechonde, ulaghitse wanangu wano weli wakale ubali wako wa kujilo na wa kumoso mne undewa wako.”
 	 22 Yesu kawalongela, “Ng'ammanyile bae achila chamlomba. Angu mwodaha kunwela ichikombe chanitsonwela nene?”
 	Wamwidika, “Twodaha.”
 	 23 Yesu kawalongela, “Mtsonwela ghendo ichikombe changu, lekeni kukala kumoso au kukala kujilo, si sang'ano yangu bae. Lekeni chinu acho watsakwing'ighwa awala iwasaghulighwe na Aba wangu.”
 	 24 Iwanang'ina kumi hawahulike apfo, tsawawonela maya awala wandughu weli.
 	 25 Lekeni Yesu kawakema, kawalongela, “Mwomanya ka iwabala we iwanu iwali si Wayahudi wowalongotsa iwanu wawo kwa ingupfu, na pfilongotsi wawo wana ukulu kuna wawo. 26 Lekeni ileke kuwa apfo kuna mwemwe, ila imunu wowose iyobama kuwa imkulu mghati mwenu, yawe mtumwa wenu, 27 na imunu wowose iyobama kuwa wa mwanduso kobamighwa yawe mtumwa. 28 Pfipfo ka Imwana we Imunu, ng'atsile bae kutumikighwa, ila kutumikila na kulapfa ughima wake kuwakombola iwanu wengi.”
 	
 Yesu kowahonetsa pfifita weli

 (Maliki 10:46-52; Luka 18:35-43)

 	29 Yesu ne iwanang'ina wake hawang'ali wakuka Yeriko, iwanu wengi tsawamuwinza. 30 Pfifita weli iwang'ali wokala mmbalimbali mwe inzila hawahulike Yesu kobita, wandusa kukemelela, “Imtwatsa, Mwana wa Daudi, utwonele libatsi!”
 	 31 Iwanu wawakembela wawalongela wanyamale, lekeni waghendelela kukemelela, “Imtwatsa, Mwana wa Daudi utwonele libatsi!”
 	 32 Yesu kema, kawakema kawaghutsa, “Mwobama niwatendele choni?”
 	 33 Wamwidika, “Imtwatsa, twobama twone!”
 	 34 Yesu kawonela libatsi, katsikinda nenge tsawo, bahala wadaha ukwona, nawo wamuwinza.
 
 Matei 21

 Yesu kakwingila Yerusalemu kwa indeng'elo

 (Maliki 11:1-11; Luka 19:28-40; Yohane 12:12-19)

 	1 Yesu ne iwanang'ina wake hawang'ali habehi na Yerusalemu na kupfika Betifage mne Chidunda cha Mitseituni, kawatuma iwanang'ina wake weli, 2 kawalongela, “Mghende mbaka mne kaye ili hambele henu, baho mtsomwona ipunda kohighwa hamwe ne imwanaghe, muwadohole mngalile hano. 3 Imunu wowose ang'awalongela chochose, mumlongele, ‘Imtwatsa kowabama,’ naye katsowaleka mke.” 4 Achino chilawila ili aghala ighalongighwe na manabii ghatimile. 5 “Umlongele neghe Sayuni,
 	Lola, Mndewa wako kokutsila,
 	Kahola na kadina ipunda, imwanapunda, imwana we ipunda.”
 	 6 Apfo iwanang'ina waghenda watenda ka Yesu pfayawalongele. 7 Wamghala ipunda ne imwana we ipunda, weka ghamaghwanda ghawo mchanya mwe punda awo, na Yesu kakala mchanya mwake. 8 Iwanu wengi wagheka ghamaghwanda ghawo mnzila na wangi waghana milala wanzasa mnzila. 9 Na iwanu iwamlongole na awala iwamuwinzile wose wandusa kukemelela, walonga, “Yatogholighwe, Imwana wa Daudi! Imulungu kambaliki ayula iyakutsa kwa taghwa lye Imtwatsa! Yatogholighwe Imulungu yali kuchanya kulanga!”
 	 10 Yesu hayengile Yerusalemu, iwanu wose wakangawala, weghutsa, “Ayu nani?”
 	 11 Iwanu wawedika, “Ayuno nabii, Yesu wa Natsareti ya Galilaya.”
 	
 Yesu mne ing'anda ye Imulungu

 (Maliki 11:15-19; Luka 19:45-48; Yohane 2:13-22)

 	12 Yesu kengila mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu kawawinga wose awala iwang'ali woghula na iwang'ali wohutsa. Katsibindula tsimetsa tsawo tsa ukubenela tsisendi na ipfighoda pfa awala iwang'ali woutsa iwanjiwa. 13 Kawalongela, “Yandikighwa, ‘Ing'anda yangu itsokemighwa ing'anda ya ukulombela.’ Lekeni mwemwe mwoitenda iwe mango ye iwabapfi!”
 	 14 Ipfifita na ipfimbete wamghendela Yesu mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu, naye kawahonetsa. 15 Lekeni iwatambika wakulu na iwolangulitsa ghamalaghitso tsawona maya hawonile pfinu pfa kukangawatsa pfayatendile Yesu, ne iwana pfawakemelele mne ing'anda ye Imulungu, “Yatogholighwe Imwana wa Daudi!” 16 Apfo wamghutsa Yesu, “Apfi kohulika chawolonga iwana wano?”
 	Kawedika, “Ona, ng'amsomile bae? ‘Kwa milomo ye iwana wadowado ne iwana iwakong'a kwotogholighwa ghendo.’ ”
 	 17 Yesu kawaleka kaghenda Betaniya, kunze kwe ghumji, kawasa kuko.
 	
 Yesu koulighita mbiki

 (Maliki 11:12-14,20-24)

 	18 Nemitondo lupfilipfili, Yesu hayang'ali kakuya mne ghumji, tsakona inzala. 19 Kaghwona mbiki mmbalimbali mwe inzila, kaghughendela lekeni ng'onile chochose bae ila imitsani iliyeka. Apfo kaghulongela, “Uleke ukweleka keli ghamatunda!” Bahala mbiki ghula ghunyala.
 	 20 Iwanang'ina wake hawonile apfo wakangawala, wamghutsa, “Ule mbiki ghuno ghusumka kunyala?”
 	 21 Yesu kawedika, “Nowalongelani ghendo mng'atoghola na kuleka kwalangula, mwodaha kutenda si achila chiliyeka ichanendile mne mbiki, ila mwodaha kuchilongela chidunda chino, ‘Wibule, wikeyase mwibahali,’ kuya itsakuwa pfipfo. 22 Mng'atoghola, chochose chamlomba mtsobokela.”
 	
 Ukulu wa Yesu woghutsighwa

 (Maliki 11:27-33; Luka 20:1-8)

 	23 Yesu kengila mne ing'anda ye Imulungu, na hayang'ali yolangulitsa, iwatambika wakulu na iwakulu we iwanu wamghendela, wamghutsa, “Kwa ukulu wachi kotenda ghano ghose? Yuhi yakwing'ile ukulu uno?”
 	 24 Yesu kawedika, “Na nene nitsowaghutsa imbuli imwe, mng'anyidika, nitsowalongela notenda ghano kwa ukulu wachi. 25 Apfi ubatitso wa Yohane ulawile kwani? Tsaulawa kulanga au kwe iwanu?”
 	Wandusa kwighutsa iwenyegho kwe iwenyegho walonga, “Tung'alonga, ‘Ulawa kulanga,’ katsotughutsa, ‘Ule lelo ng'amumtoghole Yohane?’ 26 Lekeni tung'alonga, ‘Ulawa kwe iwanu,’ twopfuka iwanu, kwaapfila wose tsawatoghola Yohane kakala nabii.” 27 Apfo wamwidika Yesu, “Ng'atumanyile bae.”
 	Naye kawedika, “Na nene siwalongela bae kwa ukulu wachi notenda ipfinu apfi.
 	
 Imbuli ye iwana weli

 	28 “Mkonatse? Imunu yumwe tsakana iwana weli, kaghenda kwa ayula mwana mkulu kamlongela, ‘Mwanangu, leloli ughende ukasang'ane mne mghunda.’ 29 Naye kamwidika, ‘Sighenda bae,’ lekeni hambele chidogho kaghaluka kaghenda. 30 Kuya aba ayo kamghendela imwana wa keli, kamlongela ichinu chichila. Naye kamwidika, ‘Ona aba,’ lekeni ng'aghendile bae. 31 Lelo yuhi mna iwana wano weli iyatendile achila chayabamile aba wake?”
 	Wamwidika, “Imwana imkulu.”
 	Yesu kawalongela, “Nowalongelani ghendo, iwasola kodi na iwaghoni watsowalongola kwingila mne undewa we Imulungu. 32 Kwaapfila Yohane tsakatsa kuwalangusa inzila inoghile, namwe ng'amumtoghole bae, lekeni iwasola kodi na iwaghoni wamtoghola. Namwe hata hamwonile apfo, ng'amghaluke bae na kumtoghola.”
 	
 Mghunda ghwa mitsabibu ne iwanu iwolima

 (Maliki 12:1-12; Luka 20:9-19)

 	33 Yesu kalonga, “Mtegheletse imbuli ingi, imunu yumwe yane ing'anda kahanda tsabibu mne mghunda. Kaghuteghela luwa mghunda agho, kahimba lipondo lya ukukamila tsabibu, katsenga ghumnala, kawakodishila iwanu iwolima, kuya koka ghumwanza. 34 Ghamatsuwa gha ukupfuna haghapfikile, kawatuma iwatumwa wake wakasole tsabibu. 35 Hawala iwanu iwolima wawaghogha iwatumwa wake, yumwe wamtowa, yungi wamkoma, na yungi wamtowa na ghamabwe. 36 Kuya tsakawatuma keli watumwa wangi, tsawengi kubita awala wamwanduso, na iwanu wala iwolima wawatendela pfipfila. 37 Hawamalile wose ghendo, kamtuma imwanaghe kuna wawo, kalonga, ‘Watsomtegheletsa mwanangu.’ 38 Lekeni iwanu iwolima hawamwonile, welongela iwenyegho, ‘Ayuno iye muhala, mtse tumkome tusole uhala wake!’ 39 Apfo wamghogha, wamwasa kunze kwe mghunda ghwe imitsabibu, wamkoma.
 	 40 “Lelo, imunu yane mghunda hayatsakutsa, yatsowatenda choni awala iwanu iwolima?”
 	 41 Wamwidika, “Katsowakoma ghendo iwanu awo wehile, katsoweka iwanu wangi mne mghunda aghwo, nawo watsomgholela tsitsabibu mne ghamatsuwa ghe kupfuna.”
 	 42 Yesu kawalongela, “Ng'amsomile bae Ghamaandiko Mahenzeluka,
 	‘Libwe ililemighwe na iwatsengagha
 	liwa libwe kulu lye lukwalambatsa.
 	Imbuli ino ilawa kwe Imulungu,
 	nayo yotukangawatsa.’
 	 43 “Apfo nowalongelani ghendo, undewa we Imulungu utsobokighwa kuna mwemwe na kwing'ighwa iwanu iwakweleka ghamatunda ghake, awala iwotenda aghala ghobama Imulungu. 44 Na ayula iyakughwa mchanya mwe libwe lino katsobeneka beneka, na wowose ilitsomghwila litsomhonda.”
 	 45 Watambika wakulu na Mafarisayo hawahulike apfo, tsawamanya Yesu tsaang'ali yowalonga wawo. 46 Apfo wabama inzila ya kumghoghela, lekeni wapfuka iwanu, kwaapfila iwanu tsawamona Yesu tsakakala nabii.
 
 Matei 22

 Imbuli ya ichihungo cha ukukwela

 (Luka 14:15-24)

 	1 Yesu kawalongela keli iwanu kwa imbuli. 2 “Undewa we Imulungu weghala ne Imndewa iyamtendele mwanaghe chihungo cha ukukwela. 3 Kawatuma iwatumwa wake wawalongele awala iwakemighwe watse kune chihungo, lekeni walema ukutsa. 4 Kuya kawatuma iwatumwa wangi, kalonga, ‘Muwalongele pfino awala iwakemighwe kune chihungo, nyambika ipfijo. Wang'ombe wangu iwanenehe wachinjighwa, na chila chinu chaghoya. Mtse kuchihungo.’ 5 Lekeni iwanu awo ng'awalangitse bae, woka, yumwe kune mghunda wake na yungi kune sang'ano tsake. 6 Nawo iwanu iwakalile wawaghogha iwatumwa wake, wawatendela pfihile na wawakoma. 7 Imndewa ayo tsakona maya. Apfo kawatuma asikali wake wawakome awala iwawakomile iwatumwa wake, na wailakatsa isi yawo. 8 Kuya kawakema iwatumwa wake kawalongela, chihungo cha ukukwela ma cha tiyali, lekeni awala iwakemighwe watse kune ichihungo ng'awatsile bae. 9 Apfo, mghende kunzila, ako wowose wamuwona muwakeme watse kune ichihungo. 10 Iwatumwa wala woka, waghenda mne tsinzila wawaghala wanu wose yawawonile, iwehile na iwanoghile, na chihungo tsachimema iwahenza.
 	 11 “Imndewa hayengile mng'anda kuwalolesa iwahenza wake, kamwona imunu yumwe, ng'apfalile bae lighwanda lye ichihungo. 12 Kamghutsa, ‘Sale yangu, angu wingiletse hano naghwe kwahela lighwanda lye ichihungo?’ Lekeni imunu ayo ng'alongile chinu bae. 13 Kuya imndewa kawalongela iwatumwa, ‘Mmwowe ghamoko na ghamaghulu mmwase kunze kune chisi. Ako kutsakuwa ne ichililo ne ukughegheda ghamatsino.’ ”
 	 14 Kuya Yesu kalonga, “Kwaapfila iwakemighwe wengi, lekeni iwasaghulighwe wadodo.”
 	
 Kuliha kodi kwa Kaisari

 (Maliki 12:13-17; Luka 20:20-26)

 	15 Apfo Mafarisayo woka na wabama inzila ye ukumtegha Yesu kwa mbuli tsake. 16 Kuya wawatuma iwanang'ina wawo hamwe ne iwanu wangi wa kingili lya Herodi. Walonga, “Mlangulitsi, twomanya ghendo ghweghwe kolongesa. Naghwe koilangulitsa pfinoghile inzila ye Imulungu, ng'upfuka bae ukulu we imunu wowose, kwaapfila ng'ulola bae ipfihanga pfe iwanu. 17 Utulongele lelo, ukonatse? Apfi pfinogha kuliha kodi kwa Kaisari, au ng'apfinoghile bae.”
 	 18 Lekeni Yesu tsakamanya ukwiha kwawo, apfo kawalongela, “Mwawang'enye, ule mwobama kunitegha? 19 Nanguseni sendi yamlihila kodi!”
 	Wamghalila isendi, 20 Naye kawaghutsa, “Angu chihanga na taghwa lino pfa nani?”
 	 21 Wamwidika, “Pfa Kaisari mndewa wa Roma.”
 	Apfo Yesu kawalongela, “Lelo, mwing'eni Kaisari aghala gha Kaisari na mwing'eni Imulungu aghala ghe Imulungu.”
 	 22 Hawahulike apfo, wakangawala, apfo wamleka, woka tsawo.
 	
 Imbuli ye ukukwela ne ukutsilihuka

 (Maliki 12:18-27; Luka 20:27-40)

 	23 Litsuwa lilyo, Masadukayo wamwenga, iwanu iwolonga kuduhu kutsilihuka, wamghendela Yesu. 24 Wamghutsa walonga, “Mlangulitsi, Musa katulongela immale ang'afa bila kweleka iwana, ndughu yake kobamighwa amkwele chitsuka ayo, ili amwelekele indughu yake iwana. 25 Lelo, hakaye hetu hano tsahana iwandughu saba. Wamwanduso kakwela, kuya kafa, na kwaapfila tsakahela iwana, mwehe wake kamlekela ndughu yake. 26 Chinu chichila chimlawila ndughu yake wa keli, wa kadatu, mbaka ndughu yake wa saba. 27 Kuya mwehe ayo naye kafa. 28 Lelo iwanu hawotsotsilihuka mne litsuwa lya kutsilihuka, mwehe ayo katsokuwa wa yuhi mna iwandughu wano saba? Kwaapfila wose tsawamkwela.”
 	 29 Yesu kawedika, “Mwakwagha, kwaapfila ng'amanyile bae Ghamaandiko Mahenzeluka au ngupfu ye Imulungu. 30 Kwaapfila iwanu hawatsotsilihuka, kuduhu ukukwela wala ukukwelighwa, watsokuwa ka malaika iwali kulanga. 31 Lekeni, imbuli yo ukutsilihuka kwe iwanu, ng'amsomile bae achila chayamlongeleni Imulungu? Kawalongela, 32 ‘Nene na Imulungu wa Abrahamu, na Imulungu wa Isaka, na Imulungu wa Yakobu.’ Yeye si Imulungu wa iwanu iwafile bae, ila Imulungu we iwanu waghima.”
 	 33 Iwanu hawahulike apfi, wakangawala kwa ghamalangulitso ghake.
 	
 Laghitso kulu

 (Maliki 12:28-34; Luka 10:25-28)

 	34 Mafarisayo hawahulike ka Yesu kawatenda Masadukayo wenyamale, wetingana hamwe, 35 yumwe wawo, imlangulitsi we Ghamalaghitso, kamghutsa Yesu kwa kumtegha. 36 Kamghutsa, “Mlangulitsi, ihi indaghitso ng'ulu kubita tsose mne Ghamaandiko Mahenzeluka?”
 	 37 Yesu kedika, “ ‘Mnoghele Imtwatsa Imulungu wako kwa ghumoyo ghwako ghose, kwa muhe wako wose, na kwa tsimbutsi tsako tsose.’ 38 Aino iyo indaghitso ng'ulu na ya mwanduso. 39 Na ya keli ighala na ino, umnoghele miyagho ka pfawinoghela imwenyegho. 40 Ghamalaghitso ghose gha Musa na ghamalangulitso ghe manabii ghohuwila Ghamalaghitso ghano meli.”
 	
 Kiristu ka Imwana wa nani?

 (Maliki 12:35-37; Luka 20:41-44)

 	41 Mafarisayo hawetingane hamwe, Yesu kawaghutsa, 42 “Mwemwe mmwonatse Kiristu. Angu imwana wa nani?”
 	Wamwidika, “Imwana wa Daudi.”
 	 43 Yesu kawaghutsa, “Ule lelo Daudi kwa kulongotsighwa na ghumuhe kamkema ‘Imtwatsa?’ Kwaapfila tsakalonga,
 	 44 ‘Imtwatsa kamlongela Imtwatsa wangu,
 	ukale hano hane ghumoko ghwangu ghwa kujilo
 	mbaka niweke iwokuhila hasi he ghamaghulu ghako.’
 	 45 Ka Daudi komkema, ‘Imtwatsa,’ lelo ikuwatse awe imwanaghe?”
 	 46 Kuduhu imunu yamwidike, na kulawa litsuwa alyo na kughendela kuduhu imunu yadahile kumghutsa Yesu imbuli yoyose.
 
 Matei 23

 Mtsoghaya

 (Maliki 12:38-39; Luka 11:43,46; 20:45-46)

 	1 Kuya Yesu kawalongela iwanu na iwanang'ina wake. 2 “Iwolangulitsa Ghamalaghitso na Mafarisayo wana ukulu wa kulangulitsa Malaghitso gha Musa. 3 Apfo mghakinde na mtende aghala ghose ghawowalongela, lekeni mleke kutenda aghala ghawotenda wawo, kwaapfila ng'awotenda bae aghala ghawolonga. 4 Wakowa imitsigho mitito na kuwatwika iwanu mmahegha mwawo. Lekeni wawo iwenyegho ng'awobama bae hata kugholosa chidole na kuinula. 5 Ghose ghawotenda, wotenda ili iwanu wawone, kwaapfila wopfala ipfinu ipfandikighwe Ghamalaghitso mne pfihanga pfawo na mne ghamoko ghawo, na wakongetsa utali we ghamaghwanda ghawo. 6 Wonoghela kukala hanu hanoghile mne chihungo na kukala mne pfighoda ipfili hambele mne tsing'anda tsa ukulombela. 7 Wonoghela kulamsighwa mmasoko na kukemighwa ne iwanu, ‘Mlangulitsi.’ 8 Lekeni mwemwe mleke kukemighwa ‘Mlangulitsi,’ kwaapfila mna Mlangulitsi yumwe yaliyeka, na mwemwe mwose mwawandughu. 9 Wala mleke kumkema imunu ‘aba’ hano muisi, kwaapfila mna ‘Aba’ yumwe yaliyeka, naye ka kulanga. 10 Na mleke kukemighwa ‘Ipfilongotsi’ kwaapfila mna ichilongotsi yumwe yaliyeka, naye Kiristu. 11 Na imkulu mghati mwenu kobamighwa yawe mtumwa wenu. 12 Na imunu wowose yetenda mkulu, katsotendighwa mdodo, na wowose yetenda mdodo, katsotendighwa mkulu.
 	
 Yesu koulighita ung'enye wawo

 (Maliki 12:4; Luka 11:39-42,44,52; 20:47)

 	13 “Mtsoghaya mwemwe yamlangulitsa Ghamalaghitso na Mafarisayo! Mwawang'enye! Kwaapfila mowahindila iwanu libani lya undewa wa kulanga, na mwemwe iwenyegho ng'amkwingila bae, wala ng'amuwalekelela awala iwobama kwingila. 14 Mtsoghaya mwemwe yamlangulitsa Ghamalaghitso na Mafarisayo! Mwawang'enye! Mwemwe mwakuja mne tsing'anda tse pfitsuka na kwa ung'enye hamlomba mwolonga mbuli nyingi! Apfo mtsohighighwa ng'ani!
 	 15 “Mtsoghaya, yamlangulitsa Ghamalaghitso na Mafarisayo! Mwawang'enye mwemwe! Mwoloka ibahali na mwakwanga mne isi yose kumtenda imunu yumwe iyaiwinze dini yenu, na ang'aghaluka, mwomtenda yawe na uwetso mala mbili wa ukwingila Jehanamu kubita mwemwe wenyegho
 	 16 “Mtsoghaya mwemwe pfilongotsi pfifita. Mwolonga, ‘Imunu ang'elaha kwe ing'anda ye Imulungu si chinu bae, ila ang'elaha kwe inzahabu ye ing'anda ye Imulungu keyowa.’ 17 Mwemwe mwawabotsi na pfifita! Chihi ichinoghile, inzahabu au ing'anda ye Imulungu iitenda inzahabu ideghete? 18 Pfipfila mwolonga, imunu ang'elaha kwa hanu hakutambikila si chinu bae, ila ang'elaha kwa nambiko iili hanu ha kutambikila, ayo keyowa. 19 Mwapfifita mwemwe! Chini chikulu nambiko au hanu ha kutambikila hakutenda nambiko ideghete? 20 Apfo ayula yelaha kwa hanu ha kutambikila, kelaha kwa chila chinu ichili mchanya mwake, 21 na ayula yelaha kwe ing'anda ye Imulungu, kelaha kwe ing'anda ayo, na kwa Imulungu iyokala mghati mwake. 22 Na ayula yelaha kwa kulanga kelaha kwa chighoda che undewa che Imulungu na kwa Imulungu iyochikalila.
 	 23 “Mtsoghaya mwemwe imlangulitsa Ghamalaghitso, na Mafarisayo! Wang'enye! Kwaapfila mwolapfa tsaka ya pfinu pfidodo ka imitsani iinung'ila ghoya, binzali na kalafuu, lekeni mwoleka kutsikinda mbuli ng'ulu tsa Ghamalaghitso ka pfila haki, libatsi ne ukutoghola. Mghatende agha, na mleke kughaleka aghala ghangi. 24 Pfilongotsi pfifita! Mwolapfa ng'onzi mne ghamatsi, lekeni mwometsa ingamiya!
 	 25 “Mtsoghaya, mwemwe yamlangulitsa Ghamalaghitso na Mafarisayo! Mwawang'enye, mwohopfugha chikombe na chiha kwa kunze, lekeni mwoleka mghati mmema ipfinu pfampatile kwa kuboka na ubwa. 26 Ghwe Mfarisayo chipfita! Tanu wopfughe mghati mwe ichikombe ne ichiha, kuya kunze kutsodegheta.
 	 27 “Mtsoghaya, mwemwe yamlangulitsa Ghamalaghitso na Mafarisayo, mwawang'enye, mwighala ne tsikabuli itsibakigwe ichokaa, kunze tsakwoneka tsinogha, lekeni mghati tsimema imipate ye iwanu iwafile na chila chinu chihile. 28 Namwe pfipfila, kunze mwakoneka kwe iwanu ka mnogha lekeni mghati mwenu, mmema ung'enye na ghehile.
 	
 Yesu kolonga Mafarisayo watsohighighwa

 (Luka 11:47-51)

 	29 “Mtsoghaya, mwemwe yamlangulitsa Ghamalaghitso, na Mafarisayo, mwawang'enye! Mowatsengela tsikabuli manabii na kutsighela unzolingo tsikabuli tse iwanu iwanoghile. 30 Namwe mwolonga, ‘Tung'akalile mne ghamatsuwa gha iwabala wetu, tung'alekile kwilunga nawo kuwakoma manabii!’ 31 Apfo mwelangusa iwenyegho ka mwa watsukulu wa awala yawawakomile manabii, 32 lelo mghendeletse achila chawatendile iwabala wenu. 33 “Mwemwe iwanzoka na iwana we iwanzoka! Mtsohepatse ukuhighighwa Jehanamu? 34 Apfo nowaghalilani manabii, ne iwanu wane nzewele, na iwalangulitsi. Wangi wawo mtsowakoma na wangi mtsowawamba mna misalaba, wangi mtsowatowa pfiboko mne tsing'anda tsenu tse ukulombela na kuwawinga kulawa ghumji ghuno kughenda ghumji ghungi. 35 Na idamu ye iwanu iwanoghile ikwitike muisi itsodaighwa kuna mwemwe, kulawa idamu ya Abeli ayula yanoghile, mbaka idamu ya Sakariya imwana wa Balakiya yamumkomile haghati he ing'anda ye Imulungu na hanu he ukulapfila inambiko. 36 Nowalongelani ghendo, mweleko ghuno ghutsohighighwa kwaajili ya agho.
 	
 Yesu kowanoghela iwanu wa Yerusalemu

 (Luka 13:34-35)

 	37 “Ghwe Yerusalemu, Yerusalemu! Ghweghwe yuwakomile manabii na kuwatowa ghamabwe awala iwatumighwe kuna ghweghwe, mala nyingi tsambama kuweka hamwe iwana wako, ka ing'uku pfowafunamila pfitsiya wake kwa ghamabawa ghake, lekeni ghweghwe, ng'aubamile bae. 38 Mlole, ing'anda yenu ye Imulungu ilekighwa uchuwa. 39 Kwaapfila nowalongelani, ng'amtsombona keli bae mbaka mlonge, ‘Kabalikighwa ayula iyakutsa kwa taghwa lye Imtwatsa.’ ”
 
 Matei 24

 Yesu kolonga kuhinyika kwe ing'anda ye Imulungu

 (Maliki 13:1-2; Luka 21:5-6)

 	1 Yesu kalawa mne ing'anda ye Imulungu, na hayang'ali yakuka, iwanang'ina wake wamghendela wamlanguse matsengo ghe ing'anda ye Imulungu, 2 Yesu kawaghutsa, “Angu mwoghona agha ghose? Nowalongelani ghendo, kuduhu libwe ilitsolekighwa mchanya mwa liyaghe, chila libwe litsokwasighwa hasi.”
 	
 Kughaya na kughanzika

 (Maliki 13:3-13; Luka 21:7-19)

 	3 Yesu hayang'ali kakala mne Chidunda cha Mitseituni, iwanang'ina wake wamghendela waliyeka wamghutsa, “Utulongele, agha ghose ghatsolawila tsuwachi? Na chihi chitsakuwa chitango cha ukutsa kwako na ukumala kwe iisi?”
 	 4 Yesu kawedika, “Mwalangitse, imunu yaleke kuwaghutsukila. 5 Kwaapfila iwanu wengi watsakutsa kwa taghwa lyangu na ukulonga wawo iwo Kiristu Imkombotsi, na watsowaghutsukila iwanu wengi. 6 Mtsohulika tsing'ondo na mbuli tsake, lekeni mleke kupfuka. Agho ghose ghobamighwa ghalawile, lekeni ukumala kwe iisi ng'ana kupfike bae. 7 Isi ingi itsetowa na isi ingi, undewa ungi witsetowa na undewa ungi. Kutsolawila inzala ng'ulu na mdedemo we isi chila hanu. 8 Agha ghose ka mwanduso wa usungu wa ukweleka imwana.
 	 9 “Kuya mtsoghoghighwa na kudunuzighwa na kukomighwa. Na isi tsose tsitsowahila kwaajili ya nene. 10 Ghamatsuwa agho iwanu wengi watsoleka ukutoghola kwawo, na watsehunduka na wetsehila, 11 na manabii wengi wa ughutsu watsolawila na kuwaghutsukila iwanu wengi. 12 Kwaajili ye ukongetseka ghehile, unoghelo we iwanu utsohunguka, 13 lekeni ayula iyodudumila mbaka utsighilo katsokombolighwa. 14 Na Imbuli ino Inoghile ya undewa itsopetighwa mne isi yose ka ukalangama kwe isi tsose, kuya ukumala kwe iisi kutsakutsa.
 	
 Ghayo kulu

 (Maliki 13:14-23; Luka 21:20-24)

 	15 “Mtsakona, ‘lideso lya ukuhinya’ lyalongile nabii Danyeli, litsakwima hanu haenzeluke, ayula iyosoma amanye. 16 Kuya iwanu iwali mne isi ya Yudeya watsumile mpfidunda. 17 Na iyali mchiswili mwe ing'anda yake, aleke kuhulumka kusola chinu chochose. 18 Yali kumghunda aleke kuya kusola lighwanda lyake. 19 Watsoghaya iwapinga wane tsiinda na awala iwakong'etsa mne ghamatsuwa agho. 20 Mlombe ili kutsuma kwenu kuleke kuwa mne msimu wa chipfeghetsi au mne litsuwa lya Sabato. 21 Kwaapfila kutsolawila maghayo ng'ana ghalawile bae kulawa isi hailumbighwe mbaka leloli, na ng'aghatsolawila keli bae. 22 Ka ghamatsuwa agho ng'aghahungusighwe bae kuduhu imunu yang'akomboke. Lekeni kwaajili ye iwanu wala iwasaghulighwe, ghamatsuwa agho ghatsohungutsighwa. 23 Imunu ang'awalongela, ‘Ulole, Kiristu Imkombotsi kahano!’ au ‘Kahala!’ mleke kutoghola. 24 Kwaapfila tsina Kiristu wa ughutsu na manabii wa ughutsu watsolawila na kutenda pfitango pfingi na pfinu pfa kukangawatsa ili kuwaghutsukila iwanu, ka yodahika hata awala iwasaghulighwe ne Imulungu. 25 Muhulikitse! Nongola kuwalongelani imbuli ino ng'ana chipindi chipfike.
 	 26 “Apfo, Imunu wowose ang'akulongela, ‘Ulole, kakunyika!’ mleke kughenda, au ‘Kahano, mne chiheleto cha mghati,’ mleke kutoghola. 27 Kwaapfila Imwana we Imunu katsakutsa ka lumwesa pfalumwemwesa mlanga mwose, kulawa ubali wa kwalilawila litsua mbaka ubali wa kwalikuswela litsua. 28 Hohose hane mtsogha, pfimanga watsetingana.
 	
 Ukutsa kwe Imwana we Imunu

 (Maliki 13:24-27; Luka 21:25-28)

 	29 “Bahala ghamatsuwa agho gha ghamaghayo aghatsomala, litsua litsoghumighwa ichisi, na lwetsi ng'alutsolapfa bae ghumwanga, tsinondo tsisolaghala kulawa mlanga na tsingupfu itsili kulanga tsitsohighisighwa. 30 Chipindi acho, chitango che Imwana we Imunu chitsolawila mlanga na isi tsose tsitsolila, iwanu watsomwona Imwana we Imunu kakutsa mna ghamawingu mlanga, hamwe ne ingupfu na utunitso mkulu. 31 Naye katsowatuma wamalaika wake wane malati ilikemela sideke, nawo watsoweka hamwe awala iwasaghulighwe kulawa chila ubali we iisi, kulawa utsighilo uno we lilanga mbaka utsighilo ungi.
 	
 Imbuli ya mkuyu

 (Maliki 13:28-31; Luka 21:29-33)

 	32 “Mwilangulitse imbuli ino kulawa mne mbiki ghwa mkuyu, ghamaputila ghake haghakuwa madeke na kwandusa kutsuka, mwomanya mvula tsahabehi. 33 Pfipfila, hamkona agha ghose mmanye chipindi cha habehi ghendo. 34 Nowalongelani ghendo, iwanu wa mweleko ghuno ng'awatsoluta bae mbaka agha ghose ghalawile, 35 lilanga ne isi pfitsoluta lekeni mbuli tsangu ng'atsitsoluta mbe.
 	
 Kuduhu imunu iyomanya litsuwa wala isaa.

 (Maliki 13:32-37; Luka 17:26-30,34-36)

 	36 “Kuduhu imunu iyomanya litsuwa wala isaa ayo, hata wamalaika wa kulanga, wala Imwana, ila Aba yaliyeka iyomanya. 37 Ka pfailawile mne ghamatsuwa gha Nuhu, itsakuwa pfipfo hayatsakutsa Imwana we Imunu. 38 Kwaapfila ghamatsuwa agho ng'ana ghamafuliko ghalawile, iwanu tsawang'ali wakuja na ukunwa, wokwela na kukwelighwa mbaka litsuwa lya Nuhu hengile mne safina. 39 Ng'awamanyile bae choni ching'alawile mbaka ghamafuliko ghatsa na kuwasola wose. Apfi pfipfo pfaitsolawila hayatsakutsa Imwana we Imunu. 40 Iwanu weli watsakuwa kumghunda, yumwe katsosolighwa na yungi katsolekighwa. 41 Iwapinga weli watsotwanga hamwe, yumwe katsosolighwa na yungi katsolekighwa.
 	 42 “Apfo, mwalangitse, kwaapfila ng'ammanya bae litsuwa lyachi Imtwatsa wenu hayatsakutsa. 43 Lekeni mmanye apfi, ka mwenye kaye ang'amanyile imbapfi kakutsa tsuwachi, ang'akalile meso, na tsang'oileka bae ing'anda yake ibenighwe. 44 Pfipfila namwe mwiyandae, kwaapfila Imwana we Imunu katsakutsa mne isaa ng'amuilolele bae yatse.”
 	
 Mtumwa yotogholighwa na yang'otogholighwa

 (Luka 12:41-48)

 	45 Yesu kaghendelela kulonga, “Kuya yuhi imtumwa yotogholighwa na yane ihekima? Ayula imtwatsa wake yamwikile yawemile iwatumwa wangi mne ing'anda yake na kuweng'a ichijo chawo chipindi chinoghile. 46 Kabweda imtumwa yula imtwatsa wake hayatsakuya na kumpfika kotenda apfo, 47 Nowalongelani ghendo, imtwatsa ayo katsomwika kwimilitsa ipfinu pfake pfose. 48 Lekeni ka mtumwa keha, na ang'elongela imwenyegho, ‘Imtwatsa wangu katsokawa kuya,’ 49 kuya kakwandusa ukuwatowa iwatumwa weyaghe na ukuja na ukunwa hamwe ne iwanu iwopatika. 50 Imtwatsa we imtumwa ayo katsakutsa mne litsuwa lyang'omlolela bae na mne isaa yang'aimanyile bae. 51 Imtwatsa ayo katsomghana pfihindi pfihindi na katsomwika hamwe ne iwang'enye, ako kutsakuwa na chililo na kughegheda ghamatsino.
 
 Matei 25

 Imbuli ye wali kumi

 	1 “Chipindi acho undewa wa kulanga witseghala ne wali kumi, iwasolile pfitasa pfawo na waghenda kumbokela imunu yokwela. 2 Watano mna wawo tsawabotsi, na watano wangi tsawana ihekima. 3 Awala wali wabotsi wosola pfitasa pfawo, lekeni ng'awasolile bae ghamafuta ghoghose. 4 Awala wane ihekima, wasola tsisupa itsimemile ghamafuta hamwe na pfitasa pfawo. 5 Imunu yokwela tsakakawa kutsa, apfo wali wose wapata nongo, wawasa. 6 “Chilo chikulu, kulawila litsi, ‘Imunu yokwela kapfika! Mlawe mkambokele!’ 7 Kuya wali wose walamka, watuwa pfitasa pfawo. 8 Awala iwabotsi wawalongela awala wane ihekima, ‘Mtugholele ghamafuta ghenu chidogho kwaapfila pfitasa pfetu pfotsimika.’ 9 Lekeni awala wane ihekima wawedika, ‘Mbe, ng'aghotwenela bae twetwe na mwemwe, ghendani kwe iwanu iwohutsa ghamafuta mkaghule.’ 10 Lekeni hawang'ali woghenda kughula ghamafuta, imunu yokwela tsakapfika. Wali awala iweyandaye, wengila naye mng'anda mne chihungo cha ukukwela. Na libani lihindighwa.
 	 11 “Hambele chidogho wali wabotsi woya, walonga, ‘Imtwatsa! Imtwatsa! Utupfughulile libani!’ 12 Lekeni kawedika, ‘Nowalongelani ghendo, siwamanyile bae.’ ”
 	 13 Kuya Yesu kalonga, “Apfo mkale meso, kwaapfila ng'ammanyile bae litsuwa au isaa.
 	
 Imbuli ye watumwa wadatu

 (Luka 19:11-27)

 	14 “Pfipfila undewa wa kulanga witseghala ne imunu iyoghenda ghumwanza, iyawakemile iwatumwa wake na kuweka wemilitse tsimali tsake. 15 Kamwing'a chila yumwe kwa kulola uwetso wake, yumwe kamwing'a mikoba mitano, yungi mikoba mili, na yungi mkoba ghumwe. Kuya koka ghumwanza. 16 Bahala imtumwa iyabokele mikoba mitano kaghenda kutsitendela sang'ano, kapata mikoba mingi mitano. 17 Pfipfila, ayula iyabokele talanta mbili tsongetseka keli talanta mbili. 18 Lekeni ayula iyabokele talanta imwe, koka kahimba hasi, kaipfisa isendi ye imtwatsa wake.
 	 19 “Ghamatsuwa pfaghalutile, imtwatsa we iwatumwa awo koya na kwandusa kupeta tsisendi hamwe nawo. 20 Imtumwa iyabokele talanta tano kamghalila talanta tano tsingi, kalonga, ‘Imtwatsa, tsakungaya talanta tano, ulole tsongetseka talanta tsingi tano.’ 21 Imtwatsa wake kamwidika, ‘Kutenda ghoya, mtumwa yunoghile na mtogholighwa! Tsakutogholighwa kwa ipfinu pfidodo, nitsokwika wimilitse pfinu pfingi. Utse udeng'elele na mtwatsa wako!’
 	 22 “Kuya imtumwa iyeng'ighwe talanta mbili naye katsa, kalonga, ‘Imtwatsa tsakungaya talanta mbili, ulole, tsongetseka tsingi mbili.’
 	 23 “Imtwatsa wake kamwidika, ‘Kutenda ghoya, imtumwa yunoghile na yutogholighwa! Tsakutogholighwa kwa pfinu pfidodo, nitsokwika wimilitse pfinu pfingi, utse na udeng'elele hamwe na mtwatsa wako!’
 	 24 “Kuya imtumwa iyabokele mkoba umwe katsa, kalonga, ‘Imtwatsa, nokumanya ghweghwe kwa imunu mkomu, kopfuna hanu ng'auhandile bae, na kokunga hanu ng'aupwililise bae tsimbeghu. 25 Apfo tsanipfuka, mbuka kupfisa isendi yako mne lidongo. Ulole, aino iyo isendi yako.’
 	 26 “Mtwatsa wake kamwidika, ‘Ghweghwe kwa imtumwa wihile na imdebwe! Tsakumanya ka nene nopfuna hanu sihandile na kukunga hanu sipwililise bae tsimbeghu. 27 Apfo tsakubamighwa kuika bengi isendi yangu, ili hambuile na nene nyambulile ifaida.
 	 28 “ ‘Mumboke sendi ayo mmwing'e ayu yane mikoba kumi. 29 Kwaapfila wowose iyalinacho, katsokongetsighwa, na wowose iyalihela chinu hata achila chayalinacho katsobokighwa. 30 Na mmwase imtumwa yuno yehile kunze mne ichisi, ako kutsakuwa na chililo na kughegheda ghamatsino.’ ”
 	
 Iwang'olo na iwamene

 	31 “Imwana we Imunu hayatsakutsa mne utunitso wake, hamwe na wamalaika, katsokala mne chighoda chake che undewa mne utunitso wa kulanga. 32 Iwanu wa kolo tsose watsetingana hambele hake, naye katsowabaghula ka iwadimi pfawowabaghula iwang'olo na iwamene. 33 Katsoweka iwanu iwanoghile kune ghumoko ghwake ghwa kujilo na iwanu wehile ghumoko ghwake ghwa kumoso. 34 Kuya Imndewa katsowalongela awala iwakalile ghumoko ghwake ghwa kujilo, ‘Mtse, mwemwe imbalikighwe na Aba wangu, mhale undewa wamwikilighwe mwemwe kulawa iisi hailumbighwe. 35 Kwaapfila tsanikala ne inzala, namwe mngaya ichijo, tsanikala ne ing'ilu, namwe mngaya ghamatsi, tsanamhenza namwe mnibokela. 36 Tsanahela lighwanda namwe mnipfetsa, tsanamtamu namwe mutsa kundola, tsanamchifungo, namwe mnyangila.’
 	 37 “Baho iwanu iwanoghile watsomwidika, ‘Imtwatsa wetu tsuwachi hatukwonile kuna inzala na tukwing'a ichijo, au kuna ing'ilu na twetwe tukwing'a ghamatsi? 38 Kuya tsuwachi hatukwonile kwa mhenza na twetwe tukubokela, au kwahela lighwanda na twetwe tukupfetsa? 39 Tsuwachi hatukwonile kwa mtamu au kwa mchifungo na twetwe tukwangila?’ 40 Imndewa katsowedika, ‘Nowalongelani ghendo, chochose chamumtendele yumwe wa wano wandughu tsangu, mnendela nene.’
 	 41 “Kuya katsowalongela awala iwali kune ghumoko ghwake ghwa kumoso, ‘Lawani hana nene, yamlighitighwe, mghende kune ghumoto ghwa ghamatsuwa ghose, ighwikighwe kwaajili ya Yehile ne malaika wake! 42 Kwaapfila tsanikala ne inzala ng'amngaile bae ichijo, tsanina ing'ilu ng'amngaile bae ghamatsi, 43 Tsanamhenza, ng'amnibokele bae, tsanahela lighwanda, ng'amnipfetse bae. Tsanamtamu na tsanamchifungo, ng'amtsile bae kumbona.’
 	 44 “Kuya nawo watsamwidika, ‘Imtwatsa, tsuwachi hatukwonile kuna inzala au kuna ing'ilu, au kwamhenza au kwahela lighwanda au kwamtamu au kwa mne chifungo, na twetwe ng'atukwapfile bae?’
 	 45 “Imndewa naye katsowedika, ‘Nowalongelani ghendo, ka tsamlema kumwapfila yumwe we iwadodo wano, tsamlema kunyapfila nene.’ 46 Kuya watsoghenda kune ukughaya kwa ghamatsuwa ghose, lekeni iwanu iwanoghile watsoghenda kune ughima wa ghamatsuwa ghose.
 
 Matei 26

 Inzila ye ukumkoma Yesu

 (Maliki 14:1-2; Luka 22:1-2; Yohane 11:45-53)

 	1 Yesu hayamalitse kulonga mbuli atso, kawalongela iwanang'ina wake, 2 “Ka pfammanya ghatsuwa meli hambele itsakuwa Pasaka, na Imwana we Imunu katsoghoghighwa ili awambighwe mna msalaba.”
 	 3 Kuya iwatambika wakulu na iwakulu watingana mne ing'anda ye imlapfa inambiko mkulu, taghwa lyake Kayafa, 4 tsawabama inzila ya kumghogha Yesu chinyelenyele wamkome. 5 Walonga, “Lekeni ileke kutendeka mne chihungo, hela kutsolawila hengele.”
 	
 Yesu kobakighwa ghamafuta ako Betaniya

 (Maliki 14:3-9; Yohane 12:1-8)

 	6 Yesu hayang'ali Betaniya mne ing'anda ya Simoni mkoma, 7 pinga yumwe kamghendela ne isupa ya alabasta iimemile ghamafuta ighonung'ila gha bei ng'ulu, kamghela mwitwi hayang'ali yakuja mmetsa. 8 Iwanang'ina hawonile apfo wona maya, waghutsa, “Angu choni kwaghitsa ghamafuta pfino?” 9 “Ghamafuta ghano ghang'autsighwe kwa bei ng'ulu, tsisendi weng'ighwe iwahingwa.”
 	 10 Yesu tsakamanya chawang'ali wolonga, kawalongela, “Ule mwomdesa ipinga ayu? Kanendela chinu chinoghile. 11 Iwahingwa mtsokala nawo ghamatsuwa ghose, lekeni ng'amtsokala bae na nene ghamatsuwa ghose. 12 Hayanighele ghamafuta ighonung'ila mlukuli mwangu, katenda apfo kuniyandaa kwa ukutsikighwa kwangu. 13 Nowalongelani ghendo, kokose imbuli inoghile haitsopetighwa mne iisi yose, chayatendile ipinga yuno chitsopetighwa kwa kumkumbuka yeye.”
 	
 Yuda kotoghola kumuhunduka Yesu

 (Maliki 14:10-11; Luka 22:3-6)

 	14 Kuya Yuda Isikarioti yumwe we awala iwanang'ina kumi na weli, kawaghendela iwatambika wakulu, 15 kawaghutsa, “Ning'awapfila ukumhunduka Yesu, mtsongaya choni?” Wampetela tsisendi selasini, wamwing'a. 16 Kulawa baho, Yuda yang'ali yobama inzila ya kumuhunduka Yesu.
 	
 Yesu kakuja ichijo che Paska ne iwanang'ina wake

 (Maliki 14:12-21; Luka 22:7-13,21-23; Yohane 13:21-30)

 	17 Mne litsuwa lye mwanduso lye Chihungo che Ipfighate ipfihela hamila, iwanang'ina wake wamghendela Yesu, wamghutsa, “Kobama tukutandile kwani ichijo che Pasaka?”
 	 18 Kawedika, “Mghende mne ghumji kwa imunu yumwe mumlongele, ‘Imlangulitsi kolonga chipindi changu chahabehi. Nene na iwanang'ina wangu tutsakuja Pasaka mng'anda mwako.’ ”
 	 19 Apfo iwanang'ina watenda ka Yesu pfayawalongele, na waitanda Pasaka.
 	 20 Nemihe haipfikile, Yesu ne iwanang'ina wake kumi na weli wakala mmetsa wakuja. 21 Hawang'ali wakuja, kawalongela, “Nowalongelani ghendo, yumwe wenu katsonihunduka.”
 	 22 Iwanang'ina tsawona usungu, chila yumwe kandusa kumlongela Yesu, “Apfi nene Imtwatsa?”
 	 23 Yesu kawalongela, “Imunu iyopfabika chighate chake hamwe na nene mne ibakuli, katsonihunduka. 24 Imwana we imunu katsokufa ka Ghamaandiko Mahenzeluka pfagholonga. Lekeni katsoghaya imunu yula iyomhunduka Imwana we Imunu. Ing'awile ng'apfu kwe imunu ka ayo ka ng'elekighwe bae.”
 	 25 Yuda, ayula iyabamile kumhunduka Yesu, kalonga, “Mlangulitsi, si nene bae.”
 	Yesu kamwidika, “Ghweghwe kulonga.”
 	
 Ichijo cha nemihe che Imtwatsa

 (Maliki 14:22-26; Luka 22:14-20; 1 Wakolinto 11:23-25)

 	26 Hawang'ali wakuja, Yesu kasola ichighate, kachibaliki, kachibena kaweng'a iwanang'ina wake, kalonga, “Msole mje, aluno lukuli Iwangu.”
 	 27 Kuya kasola chikombe, kachibaliki, kaweng'a iwanang'ina wake, kalonga, “Wose mnwele chikombe achi.” 28 “Aino iyo idamu yangu ye lilaghano, iikwitike kwaajili ya wengi kuleghusighwa nzambi. 29 Nowalongelani, sitsakunwa keli bae idipfai mbaka litsuwa lila hanitsoinwa idipfai ya sambi na mwemwe mne undewa wa Aba wangu.”
 	 30 Hawamalitse kwimba wila, woka, waghenda kune Chidunda cha Mitseituni.
 	
 Yesu kolonga Petiri katsombela

 (Maliki 14:27-31; Luka 22:31-34; Yohane 13:36-38)

 	31 Kuya Yesu kawalongela, “Chilo chino mtsotsuma na kundeka, ka pfayandikighwe.
 	Nitsomtowa imdimi,
 	na iwang'olo we likingili watsopwililika,
 	 32 Lekeni hanitsotsilihuka, nitsowalongolani Galilaya.”
 	 33 Petiri kamwidika, “Hata wose wang'akuleka, nene sikuleka bae.”
 	 34 Yesu kamlongelela Petiri, “Nokulongela ghendo, chilo chino ng'ana ijogholo yeke, kutsombela mala ndatu.”
 	 35 Petiri kamwidika, “Sikubela bae, hata ka nobamighwa nife naghwe.” Na iwanang'ina wose walonga pfipfo.
 	
 Yesu kolomba ako Getisemane

 (Maliki 14:32-42; Luka 22:39-46)

 	36 Kuya Yesu kaghenda ne iwanang'ina wake hanu hakemighwe Getisemane, kawalongela, “Mkale hano, nene noghenda hala kulomba.” 37 Kamsola Petiri na iwana weli wa Sebedayo, kuya kandusa kwona usungu, na kughanzika. 38 Kawalongela, “Ghumoyo ghwangu ghuna usungu mwingi, mbaka nobama nife. Mkale hano na mkale meso na nene.”
 	 39 Kaghenda hambele chidogho, katowa maghoti, kenama mbaka chihanga chake chighusa hasi, kalomba, “Aba wangu, ka yodahika, uchileghuse chikombe chino che maghayo kuna nene. Lekeni si ka nene pfanibama, ila ka pfaubama ghweghwe.” 40 Kuya kawoyila iwanang'ina wake, kawapfika wawasa. Kamghutsa Petiri, “Angu ng'amdahile bae kukala meso na nene hata kwa isaa imwe?” 41 “Mkale meso, mlombe ili mleke kwingila mne maghetso, ghumoyo ghwobama, lekeni lukuli lwahela ingupfu.”
 	 42 Kaghenda lwakeli, kalomba, “Aba wangu, ka ng'aidahika bae kuchileghusa ichikombe chino che maghayo mbaka nichinwe, ghoubama ghweghwe ghatendeke.”
 	 43 Hayohile lwa keli, kawapfika keli wawasa kwaapfila nenge tsawo ng'atsidahile bae kukala meso. 44 Kawaleka koka keli, na kalomba lwa kadatu, kalonga chinu chichila.
 	 45 Kuya kawoyila iwanang'ina wake kawalongela, “Angu mng'ali mwowasa na kubwihila? Mlole, isaa ya habehi, na Imwana we Imunu kakwing'ighwa kwe iwanu wane nzambi. 46 Mwinuke, tukeni! Hayo kakutsa iyonihunduka!”
 	
 Yesu koghoghighwa

 (Maliki 14:43-50; Luka 22:47-53; Yohane 18:3-12)

 	47 Hayang'ali yolonga apfo, Yuda yumwe we iwanang'ina kumi na weli, kapfika ne iwanu wengi iwakindile imimaghe ne ipfilungu, tsawatumighwa na iwatambika wakulu na iwakulu we iwanu. 48 Yuda tsakaweng'a chitango. “Imunu yanimnonela iyo yuyo yamumbama, mghogheni.”
 	 49 Bahala Yuda kamghendela Yesu, kalonga, “Mlangulitsi, nokulamsa!” Kuya kamnonela.
 	 50 Yesu kamlongela, “Sale yangu, utende achila chautsile.”
 	Kuya iwanu awo wamghendela Yesu, wamkinda, wamghogha. 51 Yumwe we awala iwakalile na Yesu kagholosa ghumoko ghwake, kasomola limaghe lyake, kamtowa imtumwa we imtambika mkulu, kamghana lighutwi.
 	 52 Yesu kamlongela, “Uyitse limaghe hanu hake, kwaapfila awala wose iwokinda limaghe watsakufa kwa limaghe. 53 Angu ng'ammanyile bae ka ning'adahile kumlomba Aba wangu, naye ang'anighalile makingili ghe asikali kubita kumi na meli ghe wamalaika watse kunyapfila. 54 Lekeni lelo ghatsotimilatse Ghamaandiko Mahenzeluka igholonga, yobamighwa ilawile pfino?”
 	 55 Bahala Yesu kawalongela iwanu wala, “Angu mutsa na mimaghe na pfilungu kungogha, ka nene na mbapfi? Chila litsuwa tsanikala namwe na nilangulitsa mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu, ng'amnighoghile bae. 56 Lekeni agha ghose ghalawila ili ghawandikile manabii ghatimile.”
 	Kuya iwanang'ina wake wamleka, watsuma.
 	
 Yesu hambele he libalatsa

 (Maliki 14:53-65; Luka 22:54-55; Yohane 18:13-14,19-24)

 	57 Awala iwamghoghile Yesu wamghala kwa Kayafa, imtambika mkulu, kwawatinganile iwolangulitsa ghamalaghitso ne iwakulu. 58 Lekeni, Petiri kamuwinza kwa kutali mbaka hachitala he mtambika mkulu. Kengila mghati, kakala hasi na iwabetetsi, yalole choni chitsolawila.
 	 59 Iwabala we inambiko na Libalatsa lyose wang'ali wobama ukalangama we ughutsu kwaajili ya Yesu, ili wadahe kumkoma. 60 Lekeni ng'awapatile ukalangama wowose bae, hata ka iwakalangama wengi we ughutsu watsa hambele.
 	Kuya iwanu weli watsa hambele, 61 walonga, “Imunu yuno kalonga apfi, ‘Nodaha kuimwagha Ing'anda ye Imulungu na kuitsenga keli mne ghamatsuwa madatu.’ ”
 	 62 Kuya mtambika mkulu kenuka kamlongela Yesu, “Kwahela che ukwidika? Agha ighawolonga iwanu wano gholongesa?” 63 Lekeni Yesu kanyamala. Mtambika mkulu, kamlongela, “Wilahe kwe Imulungu iyali mghima. Utulongele ka ghweghwe kwa Kiristu, Imwana we Imulungu.”
 	 64 Yesu kamwidika, “Ghweghwe kwolonga. Lekeni nowalongelani wose, kulawa sambi na kughendelela mtsomwona Imwana we Imunu kakala ubali wa kujilo we Imulungu Yane ingupfu, kakutsa mne ghamawingu gha kulanga.”
 	 65 Bahala Mtambika mkulu kadegha ghamaghwanda ghake kalonga, “Kaligha! Ule lelo twobama keli wakalangama? Mwemwe wenyegho mmuhulika pfayalighile. 66 Mwemwe mkonatse?”
 	Wamwidika, “Katotsa, yakomighwe.”
 	 67 Wambwalulila ghamate mchihanga na wamtowa. Wamwenga wamtowa makofi. 68 Walonga, “Ghwe Kiristu, utange yuhi yakutowile?”
 	
 Petiri kombela Yesu

 (Maliki 14:66-72; Luka 22:56-62; Yohane 18:15-18,25-27)

 	69 Petiri tsakakala kunze mwe chikuta, na imtumwa yumwe pinga kamghendela, kamlongela, “Naghwe pfipfila tsakwahamwe na Yesu wa Galilaya.”
 	 70 Lekeni Petiri kabela hambele ha wose, kalonga, “Simanyile bae chaulonga?”
 	 71 Kuya kalawa kunze, ako imtumwa yungi pinga kamwona, kuya kawalongela iwanu, “Hayuno naye tsakahamwe na Yesu wa Natsareti.”
 	 72 Petiri kabela keli, kwa kwilaha, “Simmanyile bae imunu ayo!”
 	 73 Hambele chidogho, awala iwemile hala wamghendela Petiri walonga, “Naghwe kwa yumwe wawo ghendo, kwaapfila hata kulonga kwako kolangusa ghweghwe kwa Mgalilaya.”
 	 74 Kuya Petiri kandusa kwilighita na kwilaha, kalonga, “Mbe, simmanyile bae imunu ayo!”
 	Bahala ijogholo keka, 75 na Petiri kakumbuka imbuli iyailongile Yesu. “Ijogholo ng'ana yeke, kutsombela mala ndatu.” Kalawa kunze, kalila kwa usungu.
 
 Matei 27

 Yesu koghalighwa kwa Pilato

 (Maliki 15:1; Luka 23:1-2; Yohane 18:28-32)

 	1 Nemitondotondo, iwatambika wakulu ne iwakulu we iwanu wose tsawalamla kumkoma Yesu. 2 Wamwoha, wamlongotsa wamghala kwa Pilato, mkulu wa isi iyasaghulighwe ne mkulu Roma.
 	
 Lifwa lya Yuda

 (Ghamatendo 1:18-19)

 	3 Yuda, iyamhunduke Yesu, hayonile Yesu kahighighwa, kona usungu katsuyitsa sendi tsila selasini tsayasolile kwe iwatambika wakulu. 4 Kawalongela, “Nitotsa, kwaapfila nimhunduka imunu iyalihela totso yakomighwe.”
 	Lekeni wawo wamwidika, “Twetwe ng'atukwalangula bae, alyo lyako.”
 	 5 Apfo Yuda kasa sendi atso mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu, kuya kaghenda kwikoma kwa kwibota imwenyegho. 6 Iwatambika wakulu wadondola sendi tsila, walonga, “Ng'apfinoghile bae kwika sendi tsino mne hatsina ye Ing'anda ye Imulungu. Kwaapfila atsino sendi tsa idamu.” 7 Apfo walamla sendi atso waghulile mghunda wa wafina pfiha uwe hanu he kutsikila iwahenza. 8 Ndo mana mbaka leloli mghunda awo wokemighwa, “Mghunda wa Damu.”
 	 9 Kuya achila chayalongile nabii Yeremiya chitimila, “Watsosola sendi selasini, tsawatoghole iwanu wa Isiraeli kumlihila, 10 watsitumila kughulila mghunda we wafina pfiha, ka Imtwatsa pfayanilaghitse.”
 	
 Pilato komghutsa Yesu

 (Maliki 15:2-5; Luka 23:3-5; Yohane 18:33-38)

 	11 Yesu tsakema hambele ha imkulu wa Roma, na imkulu ayo kamghutsa, “Angu ghweghwe kwa Imndewa wa Wayahudi?”
 	Yesu kamwidika, “Ghweghwe kolonga.”
 	 12 Iwabala we inambiko ne iwakulu hawang'ali womwing'a ghamaghomba, ng'edike chochose bae. 13 Kuya Pilato kamghutsa, “Angu ng'uhulika bae ghamaghomba ghano ghowokulonga?”
 	 14 Lekeni Yesu ng'edike imbuli yoyose bae, mkulu ayo kakangawala ghendo.
 	
 Yesu kohighighwa yakomighwe

 (Maliki 15:6-15; Luka 23:13-25; Yohane 18:39-19:16)

 	15 Chila chihungo che Paska imkulu wa Roma katsowela kumlekelela imwohingwa yumwe, iyawambamile iwanu. 16 Tsahana mwohighwa yumwe, iyamanyike ng'ani yakemighwe Baraba. 17 Apfo iwanu hawetingane, Pilato kawaghutsa, “Mwobama nimlekelele yuhi? Baraba au Yesu yokemighwa Kiristu?” 18 Kwaapfila Pilato tsakamanya ghendo ka wamghala Yesu kuna yeye, kwaapfila tsawamwonela chepfu.
 	 19 Pilato hayang'ali kakala mne chighoda cha kuhighila, mwehe wake kamtumila usenga, “Uleke kumtendela chochose imunu ayo yalihela totso. Kwaapfila leloli nechilo tsanidununzika ng'ani mndoto kwaajili yake.”
 	 20 Lekeni iwabala we inambiko na iwakulu, waghusongesa mtingano we iwanu wamlombe Pilato amlekelele Baraba na Yesu yakomighwe.
 	 21 Pilato kawaghutsa keli, “Yuhi mna wano weli mwombama nimlekelele?”
 	Wamwidika, “Baraba.”
 	 22 Pilato kawaghutsa, “Lelo nimtende choni ayu Yesu yokemighwa Kiristu?”
 	Wose wamwidika, “Umuwambe mna msalaba!”
 	 23 Pilato kawaghutsa, “Ule? Choni chihile chayatendile?”
 	Lekeni wose wakemelela hamwe, “Umuwambe mna msalaba!”
 	 24 Pilato hayonile ng'odaha bae chochose, ne hengele tsalyakwandusa kulawila, kasola ghamatsi, kahopfugha ghamoko ghake hambele he iwanu, kalonga, “Nene nahela litotso kwa ukufa kwe imunu ayu, alyo lyenu iwenyegho!”
 	 25 Iwanu wose walonga, “Totso lye ukufa kwake liwe mchanya mwetu na mchanya mwe iwanetu!”
 	 26 Kuya kamlekelela Baraba kuna wawo. Lekeni kalonga wampfapule Yesu na mijeledi, kamlapfa yawambighwe mna msalaba.
 	
 Asikali wombetsa Yesu

 (Maliki 15:16-20; Yohane 19:2-3)

 	27 Kuya asikali wa Pilato wamghala Yesu mne ing'anda ye imndewa, na kingili lyose lye asikali limmemela. 28 Wamtsula ghamaghwanda ghake, wampfatsa lighwanda dung'u, 29 Kuya wabota fiya ya tsimiwa walika mwitwi mwake, kuya weka ing'weku mne ghumoko ghwake wa kujilo, watowa ghamaghoti hambele hake. Wambetsa, walonga, “Mbukwa, Imndewa wa Wayahudi.” 30 Wambwalulila ghamate, wasola ing'weku wamtowa mwitwi. 31 Hawamalitse kumbetsa, wamtsula lighwanda alyo, wampfatsa ghamaghwanda ghake. Wamghala yawambighwe mna msalaba.
 	
 Yesu kowambighwa mna msalaba

 (Maliki 15:21-32; Luka 23:26-43; Yohane 19:17-27)

 	32 Hawang'ali wakuka, watingana ne imunu yumwe iyolawila Kirene, iyakemighwe Simoni, wamnanahitsa yaughale msalaba. 33 Wapfika hanu hokemighwa Goligota, mana yake Chibombwe che Litwi. 34 Wamwing'a Yesu idipfai iitifighwe ne ichinu che usungu, lekeni hayailanzile, kalema ukunwa.
 	 35 Wamuwamba mna msalaba, kuya wegholela ghamaghwanda ghake kwa kutowa simbi. 36 Wakala hasi wamlolesa. 37 Na hachanya he litwi lyake, wandika lighomba lyake, “Ayuno Yesu, Imndewa wa Wayahudi.” 38 Iwabapfi weli nawo tsawawambighwa hamwe naye, yumwe ghumoko ghwake ghwa kujilo na yungi ghumoko ghwake ghwa kumoso.
 	 39 Iwanu iwalutile hala, wahighitsa ghamatwi ghawo kwa kumbetsa, wamligha, 40 walonga, “Ambe ghweghwe ung'aimwaghile Ing'anda ye Imulungu na kuitsenga keli mne ghamatsuwa madatu! Lelo wikombole imwenyeng'o. Ka ghweghwe kwa Imwana we Imulungu hulumka mna msalaba.”
 	 41 Pfipfila iwatambika wakulu na iwolangulitsa ghamalaghitso, na iwabala wose wambesa. 42 Walonga, “Kawakombola iwanu wangi, lekeni ng'odaha bae kwikombola imwenyegho, ambe yeye ka Imndewa we Isiraeli, tumlole lelo yahulumke mna msalaba, na twetwe tutsomtoghola. 43 Tsakamuhuwila Imulungu na kalonga ‘Nene na Imwana we Imulungu.’ Lekani lelo tulole Imulungu yamkombole ka kombama.”
 	 44 Pfipfila iwabapfi weli iwawambighwe hamwe naye, wamligha.
 	
 Ukufa kwa Yesu

 (Maliki 15:33-41; Luka 23:44-49; Yohane 19:28-30)

 	45 Kulawa saa sita mbaka saa tisa ichisi tsachighubika isi yose. 46 Haipfikile saa tisa, Yesu kakemelela, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabakitani?” Mana yake, “Imulungu wangu, Imulungu wangu, ebali kondeka?”
 	 47 Iwanu iwemile hala hawahulike apfo, walonga, “Komkema Eliya.”
 	 48 Bahala yumwe wawo katsuma kasola dodoki, kalika mne dipfai iing'ang'a, kuya kalika mne ing'weku kamwing'a Yesu yainwe. 49 Awala iwanu wangi walonga, “Lelo mleke tulole ka Eliya kakutsa kumkombola.”
 	 50 Yesu kakemelela keli kwa litsi likulu, kuya kafa.
 	 51 Bahala lipatsiya ililimghati mwe Ing'anda ye Imulungu lidegheka pfihindi pfibili kulawa uchang'a mbaka hasi. Isi tsaidedema na ghamabambalawe ghatulika. 52 tsikabuli tsighubuka ne iwanu wengi we Imulungu iwafile tsawatsilihuka. 53 Walawa kunze mwe tsikabuli, na Yesu hayatsilihuke waghenda mne ghumji mwenzeluka, na iwanu wengi wawona.
 	 54 Ayula imkulu we asikali na awala iwakalile naye womkalitsa Yesu, hawonile isi ihighisika na ghose ighalawile, tsawapfuka, walonga, “Ayuno tsa Imwana we Imulungu ghendo!”
 	 55 Tsakukala na iwapinga wengi, wololesa kwa kutali, awo iwo iwamuwinzile Yesu kulawa Galilaya na iwamwapfile. 56 Mna wawo, tsakukala na Mariya Magidalena, Mariya mai wawo tsina Jakobu na Yosefu na mai we iwana wa Sebedayo.
 	
 Kutsikighwa kwa Yesu

 (Maliki 15:42-47; Luka 23:50-56; Yohane 19:38-42)

 	57 Nemihe haipfikile, imunu yumwe tajiri kulawa Arimataya iyakemighwe Yosefu kapfika, naye imwenyegho tsakakala mwanang'ina wa Yesu. 58 Kamghendela Pilato kamlomba yamwing'e lukuli lwa Yesu, na Pilato kalaghitsa yeng'ighwe. 59 Yosefu kalusola lukuli, kalupfatsa isanda inoghile, 60 kalwika hanu hake imwenyegho ha sambi ha kutsikila. Kuya kabingilisa libwe kulu hambele he libani lye likabuli, kuya koka. 61 Mariya Magidalena na Mariya yungi tsawakala baho, welolesa ne likabuli.
 	
 Asikali hane likabuli

 	62 Litsuwa lya keli, ilili litsuwa lya Sabato, iwatambika wakulu na Mafarisayo waghenda kwa Pilato. 63 Walonga, “Imndewa, twokumbuka mghutsu yula, hayang'ali mghima tsakalonga, ‘Ghang'abita ghamatsuwa madatu, nitsotsilihuka keli.’ 64 Apfo, ulaghitse kabuli lyake walikalitse ghoya mbaka mne litsuwa lya kadatu. Hela iwanang'ina wake wodaha kutsa na kulwiba lukuli lwake na kuwalongela iwanu kuwa katsilihuka. Ughutsu uno wa utsighilo utsakuwa wiha kubita ula wa mwanduso.”
 	 65 Pilato kawedika, “Mnawo asikali, mghende mkakalitse likabuli ka pfamdaha.”
 	 66 Apfo woka na wakalitsa ghoya likabuli kwa kwika chitango mne libwe na wawaleka asikali wokalitsa.
 
 Matei 28

 Kutsilihuka kwa Yesu

 (Maliki 16:1-10; Luka 24:1-12; Yohane 20:1-10)

 	1 Litsuwa lya Sabato halimalile, lupfilipfili litsuwa lye mwanduso lye lijuma, Mariya Magidalena na Mariya yungi waghenda kulola likabuli.
 	 2 Tsakulawila mdedemo mkulu we isi, kwaapfila malaika we Imtwatsa tsakahulumka kulawa kulanga, kaghenda mne likabuli kalibingilisa libwe hambali, kalikalila. 3 Chihanga chake tsachikala ka lumwesa, na lighwanda lyake tsalitselu chwee! 4 Iwanu iwang'ali wokalitsa wapfuka ghendo, wadedema na woneka ka wafa.
 	 5 Malaika ayo kawalongela iwapinga, “Mleke kupfuka, kwaapfila nomanya mwombama Yesu iyawambighwe mna msalaba. 6 Ng'alibaha bae, katsilihuka ka pfayalongile. Mtse mlole hanu hayawasile. 7 Lelo msumke mghende, muwalongelele pfino iwanang'ina wake. ‘Yesu katsilihuka, naye katsowalongola kughenda Galilaya. Baho mtsomwona.’ Haya lelo, ma niwalongela.”
 	 8 Apfo iwapinga awo wasumka kuka kulawa hane likabuli, kwa kupfuka na ndeng'elelo ng'ulu, watsuma waghenda kuwalongela iwanang'ina wake.
 	 9 Bahala Yesu ketingana nawo, kawalongela, “Nowalamsani.” Wamghendela, wakinda ghamaghulu ghake, wamtamanila. 10 Kuya Yesu kawalongela, “Mleke kupfuka. Mghende mkawalongele wandughu tsangu waghende Galilaya, ako watsombona.”
 	
 Iwakalitse likabuli wolonga ichilawile

 	11 Iwapinga hawang'ali wamnzila, asikali wangi mna awala iwakalitse likabuli waghenda kune ghumji wawalongela watambika wakulu chila chinu ichilawile. 12 Iwakulu we inambiko hawetingane ne iwabala wapanga imbuli yawo, waweng'a sendi nyingi awala iwakalitse likabuli, 13 kuya wawalongela, “Walongeleni pfino iwanu, ‘Iwanang'ina wake watsa nechilo, wamwiba hatuwasile.’ 14 Na imkulu we isi ang'ahulika mbuli ino, twetwe tutsolonga naye, namwe ng'amtsokwingila mne maghayo.”
 	 15 Apfo awala asikali wasola sendi, na watenda ka pfawalongelighwe. Na mbuli ayo yenela kwe Wayahudi mbaka leloli.
 	
 Laghitso kulu

 (Maliki 16:14-18; Luka 24:36-49; Yohane 20:19-23; Ghamatendo 1:6-8)

 	16 Kuya iwanang'ina kumi na yumwe waghenda Galilaya kune chidunda, ako Yesu kwayawalongele waghende. 17 Hawamwonile, wamtamanila lekeni wangi wapfuka. 18 Yesu kawaghendela, kawalongela, “Ukulu wose uli kulanga na uli muisi ning'ighwa nene. 19 Apfo, mghende mkawatende iwanu we isi tsose wawe wanang'ina wangu, muwabatitse kwa taghwa lya Aba na Imwana na Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka, 20 na muwalangulitse kughakinda aghala ghose ghaniwalaghitse. Na nene na hamwe namwe ghamatsuwa ghose mbaka iisi haitsomala.”
 
 Ghamatendo 1

 	1 Kuna imkulu Teofili,
 	Mne ichitabu changu chanongole ukwandika, tsanyandika ipfinu pfose Yesu pfatendile na pfayalangulitse, kulawa handuse isang'ano yake 2 mbaka litsuwa lila hayasolighwe kughenda kulanga. Ichipindi ng'ana yasolighwe, tsakaweng'a malaghitso kwa uwetso wa Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka iwatumighwa wala iyawasaghule. 3 Matsuwa alubaini kulawa hafile, Yesu kawalawila mala nyingi na kwilangusa ghendo ka tsakakala mghima. Wamwona, naye kalonga nawo mbuli tse Undewa we Imulungu. 4 Na litsuwa limwe, hayang'ali yakuja nawo kawalaghitsa pfino, “Mleke kulawa Yerusalemu, ila mwemwe mbete achila chayalongile Aba, iyo Ghumuhe yamnihulike nomlonga. 5 Yohane tsakabatitsa kwa ghamatsi, lekeni matsuwa chidogho ighakutsa, mtsobatitsighwa kwa Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka.”
 	
 Yesu kosolighwa kulanga

 (Maliki 16:19-20; Luka 24:50-53)

 	6 Iwatumighwa hawetingane na Yesu, wamghutsa, “Imtwatsa, pfii matsuwa ghano kutsowoyitsila Waisiraeli Undewa?”
 	 7 Yesu kawalongela, “Matsuwa na msimu pfamne uwetso wa Aba wangu, mwemwe ng'ambamighwa bae kumanya itsakuwa tsuwachi. 8 Lekeni Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka hatsowahulumkila, mtsobokela ingupfu, namwe mtsakuwa iwakalangama wangu ako Yerusalemu, mne tsiisi tsa Yudeya na Samariya, na muisi mwose.” 9 Hayamalitse kulonga apfo kasolighwa kulanga, aku wose womlola, kuya liwingu limghubika nawo ng'awamwonile keli bae.
 	 10 Hawang'ali wotsodola tsinenge kulanga Yesu hang'ali yakuka, bahala iwanu weli iwapfalile maghwanda matselu wema habehi yawo, 11 walonga, “Mwemwe iwanu wa Galilaya! Ebali mwima hano mwolola kulanga? Yesu yuyuno, iyasolighwe kuna mwemwe kughenda kulanga, katsakuya keli ka pfipfo pfammwonile kakuka kulanga.”
 	
 Matiasi kosaghulighwa akinde hanu ha Yuda

 	12 Kuya iwatumighwa woya Yerusalemu kulawa mne Chidunda cha Mitseituni, utali wa chilomita ka imwe kulawa mkaye. 13 Hawapfikile mkaye, wengila mne chiheleto cha kuchanya chawang'ali wokalagha. Nawo tsawakala Petiri, Yohane, Yakobu, Andereya, Filipi, Tomasi, Batalomeyo, Matei, Jakobu imwana we Alifayo, Simoni Mkanani na Yuda mwanaghe Jakobu. 14 Awo wose tsawaghendelela kwitingana hamwe ukulomba, hamwe ne iwapinga wangi, na Mariya mai wake Yesu, na ndughu tsake Yesu.
 	 15 Litsuwa limwe mne matsuwa agho, Petiri kema haghati he iwanu iwetingane. Tsawakala iwanu miya imwe na ishilini. 16 Petiri kalonga, “Ndughu tsangu, tsaibamighwa Ghamaandiko Mahenzeluka ghatimile. Ghumwande Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka tsakalonga kubitila Daudi, Daudi tsakatabili mbuli tsa Yuda, iyawalongotse iwanu wala iwamghoghile Yesu. 17 Yuda tsakakala miyetu kwaapfila tsakasaghulighwa na Yesu tusang'ane naye.”
 	 18 Yeye tsakaghula mghunda kwa sendi tsapatile kwa sang'ano yake ila ihile, kaghwa hamo, katulika na usapi wake wose ulawa kunze. 19 Iwanu wose wa Yerusalemu tsawahulika mbuli atso, apfo mne chilugha chawo waghukema mghunda aghwo Akelidama, mana yake “Mghunda ghwe Idamu.”
 	 20 Petiri kalonga, “Kwaapfila yandikighwa mne Tsaburi,
 	‘Ing'anda yake ikale uchuwa,
 	imunu wowose aleke kukala mng'anda amwo.’ Pfipfila yandikighwa,
 	‘Imunu yungi yeng'ighwe isang'ano yake ya kulongotsa.’
 	 21 “Apfo yobamighwa kumsaghula imunu yumwe kulawa mne iwanu iwelongotse na twetwe matsuwa ghose Imtwatsa Yesu hayang'ali na twetwe, 22 kulawa Yohane hayang'ali yobatitsa mbaka litsuwa lila Yesu hayasolighwe kulawa kuna twetwe kughenda kulanga. Imunu ayo kobamighwa yawe mkalangama miyetu wa kutsilihuka kwa Yesu.”
 	 23 Apfo wasaghula mataghwa meli, Yosefu iyakemighwe Barisaba, pfipfila tsakakemighwa Yusti, na wa keli Matiasi. 24 Kuya walomba, “Imtwatsa, ghweghwe kwoimanya imimoyo ye iwanu wose. Lelo utulanguse, imunu yuhi yumsaghule mne iwanu wano weli 25 ili asole isang'ano ye utumighwa yailekile Yuda na kughenda hanu hake imwenyegho.” 26 Kuya watowa simbi, na simbi imghwila Matiasi, naye kongetsighwa mne iwatumighwa wala kumi na yumwe.
 
 Ghamatendo 2

 Ukutsa kwa Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka

 	1 Litsuwa lya Pentekoste halipfikile, wose iwamtoghole Yesu tsawetingana hanu hamwe. 2 Bahala, iwanu wahulika chinu choduma kulawa kulanga ka beho liduma kwe ingupfu, limemesa ing'anda yose iwakalile iwanu awo. 3 Kuya, pfilawila ipfinu ipfikoneka ka milambi ya ghumoto, napfo pfipwililika na kukala mchanya mwa chila imunu. 4 Wose tsawamemesighwa Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka, wandusa kulonga lugha tsingi ka Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka pfayawatendile wadahe kulonga.
 	 5 Ako Yerusalemu tsakukala na Wayahudi iwompfuka Imulungu iwalawile chila isi. 6 Hawahulike litsi alyo, iwanu wetingana hamwe. Wose wakangawala kwaapfila chila imunu kawahulika wolonga kwa chilugha chake imwenyegho. 7 Wakangawala ng'ani, walonga, “Pfii, iwanu wano wose watuwahulika wolonga pfino, si Wagalilaya bae? 8 Ebali lelo, chila imunu mna twetwe kowahulika wolonga chokaye? 9 Wamwenga twolawila Paritiya, Midiya na Elamu, wamwenga wolawila Mesopotamiya, Yudeya, Kapadokiya, Ponto na isi ya Asiya, 10 Na wamwenga wolawa Firigiya, Pamfiliya, Misiri na kaye tsa Libiya tsili habehi na Kirene, wamwenga wetu wolawila Roma, 11 na Wayahudi ne iwanu iwengile mne dini ya Chiyahudi, wamwenga wolawila Kirete ne Arabiya. Twetwe wose twowahulika wolonga ipfinu pfikulu pfayatendile Imulungu kwa lugha tsetu iwenyegho.” 12 Wose wakangawala, wapfuka, weghutsa, “Achi nacho choni?”
 	 13 Lekeni iwanu wangi wawabetsa, walonga, “Iwanu wano wapatika!”
 	
 Petiri Kolonga ne Wanu

 	14 Kuya Petiri kema nawo iwatumighwa wala kumi na yumwe, kandusa kuwalongela iwanu awo kwa kukemelela, “Wayahudi weyangu, na mwemwe mwose yamkala hano Yerusalemu, mleke niwalongele, namwe mtegheletse ghoya chanilonga. 15 Iwanu wano ng'awapatike bae ka pfamlonga. Sambi saa tatu nemitondo! 16 Achino ichilawile chicho chayalongile Yoeli, nabii we Imulungu,
 	 17 ‘Imulungu kolonga, mne matsuwa gha utsighilo
 	nitsowamwaghila iwanu wose Ghumuhe ghwangu.
 	Iwana wenu na neghe tsenu watsopeta mbuli yangu,
 	iwasongolo wenu watsakona ghamaono,
 	ne iwabala wenu watsolota tsindoto.
 	 18 Hata iwatumwa wangu pfipfila, wose iwamale ne iwapinga
 	nitsowamwaghila Ghumuhe ghwangu mne matsuwa agho,
 	nawo watsopeta mbuli yangu.
 	 19 Nitsotenda pfihulo uchanya kulanga,
 	ne ipfinu pfa ukukangawatsa muisi,
 	kutsakuwa na idamu, ghumoto na hosi tito.
 	 20 Litsua litsoghaluka kuwa chisi,
 	na lwetsi lutsakuwa ludung'u ka idamu,
 	aho ng'ana lipfike litsuwa lila likulu lye utunitso we Imtwatsa.
 	 21 Ne imunu wowose iyatsolomba kwa taghwa lye Imtwatsa katsokombolighwa.’
 	 22 “Iwanu we Isiraeli, mtegheletse imbuli ino! Yesu wa Natsareti tsakakala imunu yane uwetso iyalangusighwe kuna mwemwe kwe pfihulo, pfinu pfa kukangawatsa ne ipfitango pfatendile Imulungu kuna mwemwe kubitila yeye, ka mwemwe iwenyegho pfammanya. 23 Kulawa mwanduso Imulungu imwenyegho tsakabama Yesu aghoghighwe na mwemwe, namwe mumkoma kwa kuwaleka iwanu wehile wamuwambe mna msalaba. 24 Lekeni Imulungu kamtsiliula Yesu, kamkombola kulawa mne usungu we lifwa kwaapfila ng'aidahike bae lifwa limwohe. 25 Mana Daudi tsakalonga pfino mbuli tsa Yesu,
 	‘Tsanimwona Imtwatsa hambele hangu matsuwa ghose
 	Kwaapfila yeye ka habehi hangu
 	Sitsohighisika bae.
 	 26 Apfo, ghumoyo ghwangu ghwodeng'elela,
 	lulimi lwangu lolonga kwa kudeng'elela,
 	na lukuli lwangu lutsokala kwa lolelo,
 	 27 kwaapfila ng'utsondeka kutsimu bae,
 	ng'utsomleka bae Mwenzeluka wako yole mne likabuli.
 	 28 Kunilangusa inzila ye ughima,
 	kutsonimemesa ndeng'elo kwaapfila kwa hamwe na nene.’
 	 29 “Wandughu, ndekeni nonge mwatsimwatsi mbuli tsa aba wetu mkulu Daudi. Yeye kafa, katsikighwa na likabuli lyake lyabahano mbaka leloli. 30 Lekeni kwaapfila Daudi tsakakala nabii we Imulungu, kamanya ka Imulungu kelaha kuna yeye ka ang'amtendile mtsukulu wake yumwe yawe imndewa ka pfayakalile Daudi. 31 Daudi tsakalongola kughona agho ighatsotendighwa ne Imulungu, apfo kalonga mbuli tse ukutsilihuka kwa Kiristu Mkombotsi, hala hayalongile,
 	‘Ng'alekighwe kutsimu bae,
 	wala lukuli lwake ng'alolile bae.’
 	 32 “Imulungu iyo yamtsilihule ayo Yesu, na twetwe twa iwakalangama we chinu acho. 33 Naye Yesu henulighwe na kwikighwa lubali lwa kujilo lwe Imulungu, kabokela Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka kulawa kwa Aba wake ka pfayatulongele. Kuya katughalila Ghumuhe ayo, na acho chicho chamchona sambi na kuchihulika. 34 Kwaapfila si Daudi bae iyasolighwe kughenda kulanga, ila yeye kalonga,
 	‘Imtwatsa kamlongela Imtwatsa wangu,
 	ukale hano hane ubali wangu wa kujilo
 	 35 mbaka niwatende wehile wako
 	wawe hasi ha ghamaghulu ghako.’
 	 36 “Apfo iwanu wose wa Isiraeli wobamighwa wamanye ghendo, Imulungu kamtenda ayu Yesu imumuwambile mna msalaba yawe Imtwatsa na Kiristu Mkombotsi.”
 	 37 Iwanu hawahulike agho, ghawahoma ghendo mmoyo, wawaghutsa Petiri na iwatumighwa wangi, “Ndughu tsetu, lelo tutendatse?”
 	 38 Petiri kawedika, “Chila imunu yatsileke nzambi tsake, mbatitsighwe kwa taghwa lya Yesu Kiristu, na Imulungu katsomleghusilani nzambi tsenu. Namwe mtsobokela laghano lye Imulungu, iyo Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka. 39 Kwaapfila laghano lila tsamwikilighwa mwemwe, na iwana wenu, na iwanu wose iwali kutali na awala wose iwatsokemighwa ne Imtwatsa Imulungu wetu.”
 	 40 Kwa mbuli nyingi Petiri kawakomangitsa iwanu, kalonga, “Mwikombole kulawa mweleko ghuno ghuhile.” 41 Iwanu wengi watsitoghola mbuli tsake, wabatitsighwa. Mne litsuwa lila, iwanu ka 3,000 wongetseka. 42 Awo wose waghendelela kulangulitsighwa ne iwatumighwa wa Yesu, wakala hamwe ka iwandughu, wamegha ichighate na walomba hamwe.
 	
 Pfawakalile awala iwamtoghole Yesu

 	43 Iwatumighwa tsawatenda pfihulo na pfinu pfa kukangawatsa pfingi, chila imunu ang'ali yopfuka. 44 Iwatoghole wose waghendelela kukala hamwe na kwigholela ipfinu pfawo. 45 Tsawang'ali wohutsa mali tsawo ne ipfinu pfawo na kwigholela sendi ka chila imunu pfayabamile. 46 Waghendelela kwitingana mne ing'anda ye Imulungu chila litsuwa. Lekeni hawang'ali womegha chighate, tsawetingana mne tsing'anda tsawo na ukuja ichijo acho kwa ndeng'elo na ghumoyo mtselu. 47 Tsawamtunitsa Imulungu ne iwanu wose wanoghelesighwa nawo. Na chila litsuwa Imtwatsa yang'ali yowongetsela iwanu iwang'ali wokombolighwa.
 
 Ghamatendo 3

 Petiri na Yohane womhonetsa ichimbete

 	1 Litsuwa limwe, Petiri na Yohane wang'ali woghenda mne ing'anda ye Imulungu saa tisa nemisi, iwanu hawoghendagha kulomba. 2 Iwanu tsawang'ali womghalagha imunu yumwe iyakalile chimbete kulawa kwelekighwa kwake. Chila litsuwa iwanu wang'ali womwika imunu ayo mne libani lye ing'anda ye Imulungu ilikemighwe “Libani linoghile” ili yalombe chochose kwe iwanu iwang'ali wakwingila mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu. 3 Hayawonile Petiri na Yohane wakwingila mng'anda, kawalomba wamwing'e chochose. 4 Nawo wamtsodolela tsinenge. Kuya Petiri kamlongela, “Tulolese!” 5 Naye kawalola, kalolela kupata ichinu chochose kulawa kuna wawo. 6 Lekeni Petiri kamlongela, “Nahela sendi, ila nokwing'a achila chanili nacho, kwa taghwa lya Yesu Kiristu wa Natsareti, winuke ughende!” 7 Kuya kamkinda ghumoko ghwake ghwa kujilo, kamwapfila ukwinuka, bahala ghamaghulu, na mbweghele tse imunu ayo tsiwa na ngupfu. 8 Kadaluka kwa ghamaghulu ghake na kwandusa ukughenda. Kuya kengila nawo mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu, koghenda kodaluka daluka aku komtunya Imulungu. 9 Iwanu wose hawamwonile koghenda na komtunya Imulungu, 10 wamtanga yeye kayuyula iyang'ali yolomba habehi na “Libani linoghile” lye Ing'anda ye Imulungu, weduka, wakangawala kwa achila ichimlawile.
 	
 Mbuli tsa Petiri mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu

 	11 Imunu ayo hang'ali yoghenda na Petiri na Yohane, iwanu wose wang'ali wokangawala na wandusa kutsumila hanu ha kwitinganila hakemighwe “Ukumbi wa Selemani.” 12 Petiri honile apfi, kawalongela, “Iwanu wa Isiraeli, ebali mwokangawala kwe ichinu chino? Mbona mwotutsodolela tsinenge ka twetwe itumtendile imunu yuno yadahe kughenda kwa ngupfu tsetu iwenyegho au kwaapfila tunogha hambele he Imulungu? 13 Imulungu wa Abrahamu, Isaka na Yakobu, Imulungu we iwabala wetu, tsakamtunya Yesu imtumighwa wake, ila mwemwe mumghogha ili yakomighwe, namwe mumlema hambele ha Pilato, lekeni Pilato tsakabama yamlekelele yoke. 14 Tsakakala Mwenzeluka na imunu yanoghile, lekeni mwemwe mumlema, mumlomba Pilato yamlekelele imunu iyakomile. 15 Mwemwe mumkoma yeye yali mwanduso wa ughima, lekeni Imulungu kamtsilihula kulawa mne lifwa, na twetwe twa wakalangama we ichinu acho. 16 Kwa kutoghola taghwa lya Yesu, imunu ayu immwona na imummanya keng'ighwa ingupfu. Ukutoghola na taghwa lya Yesu pfimhonetsa ghendo imunu ayu ka wose pfammwona.
 	 17 “Lelo ndughu tsangu, nomanya ka mwemwe ne iwakulu wenu mghatenda agho kwaapfila ng'ammanyile bae. 18 Lekeni Imulungu katimitsa achila chayalongile ghumwande kubitila manabii wose we Imulungu, ka ibamighwa Kiristu wake yadununzike. 19 Lelo mtsileke nzambi tsenu mmuyile Imulungu, ili yawaleghusile nzambi tsenu. Mng'atenda apfo, 20 mtsakongetsighwa ngupfu tsa muhe kulawa kwe Imtwatsa, naye katsomtuma Yesu Kiristu, iyamsaghulileni. 21 Kobamighwa akale kulanga mbaka ichipindi che Imulungu kutenda ipfinu pfose pfiwe pfa sambi chipfike, ka pfayalongile ghumwande kubitila manabii wake wahenzeluka. 22 Kwaapfila Musa tsakalonga, ‘Imtwatsa Imulungu wenu katsomghalileni nabii wake ka pfanighalile nene, ayo katsolawila mghati mwenu mwenyegho, mwobamighwa muhulikitse chila ichinu chayowalongela. 23 Imunu wowose iyolema kumuhulikitsa nabii ayo, katsobaghulighwa kulawa kwe iwanu we Imulungu na katsokomighwa.’ 24 Wanabii wose we Imulungu, kwanzila Samweli na awala iwatsile hambele, tsawalonga mbuli tse ipfinu ipfilawila mne matsuwa ghano. 25 Imulungu tsakawalapfila mwemwe laghano kubitila wanabii we Imulungu, namwe mwamghati mwa laghano lila lyatendile Imulungu ne iwabala wenu, ka pfayamlongele Abrahamu, ‘Kubitila mweleko ghwako, nitsowabaliki iwanu wose muisi mwose.’ 26 Imulungu hayamtsilihule imtumighwa wake, tanu kamtumilani mwemwe, yawabaliki na yamtende chila yumwe wenu aleke kutenda ghehile.”
 
 Ghamatendo 4

 Petiri na Yohane woghalighwa mne libalatsa

 	1 Petiri na Yohane hawang'ali wowalongela iwanu, iwatambika wakulu ne iwakulu wa wakalitsa Ing'anda ye Imulungu hamwe na Masadukayo tsawapfika. 2 Tsawona maya ng'ani kwaapfila iwatumighwa awo wang'ali wolangulitsa iwanu ka Yesu katsilihuka, ichinu ichikonesa ghendo ka iwanu iwafile watsotsilihuka. 3 Apfo wawaghogha Petiri na Yohane, waweka mwigheletsa mbaka ilupfi yake, kwaapfila tsaikala nemihe. 4 Lekeni iwanu wengi iwahulike imbuli yawailongile Petiri na Yohane watoghola, na iwanu iwatoghole tsawongetseka na kuwa ka iwanu elufu tano.
 	 5 Litsuwa liwinzile, iwakulu wa Wayahudi, iwabala ne iwolangulitsa Ghamalaghitso wetingana hamwe ako Yerusalemu. 6 Tsawetingana ne Imtambika mkulu Anasi, Kayafa, Yohane, Alekisanda na iwanu wangi wa lukolo lwa Imtambika mkulu. 7 Tsawaweka hambele hawo, wawaghutsa, “Mwemwe mtenda ichinu chino kwa ingupfu yachi na kwa taghwa lya nani?”
 	 8 Kuya Petiri, aku kamema Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka, kawedika, “Mwemwe iwakulu ne iwabala we iwanu! 9 Mng'atughutsa leloli kwa chinu chila chinoghile chayatendelighwe imunu yula chimbete, na pfahonile, 10 iwanu wose wa Isiraeli mwobamighwa mmanye ka imunu ayu iyemile hano hambele henu, kamghima ghendo kwe ingupfu ya taghwa lya Yesu Kiristu wa Natsareti, yula imumuwambile mna msalaba na Imulungu iyamtsilihule kulawa mne lifwa. 11 Yesu iyo
 	‘Libwe lyamlemile mwemwe iwatsenga ng'anda,
 	sambi liwa libwe kulu lya ukwalambatsa.’
 	 12 Yeye yaliyeka iyodaha kuwakombola iwanu, kwaapfila mne isi yose kuduhu taghwa lyatwing'ighwe twetwe tukombolighwe nalyo.”
 	 13 Iwabala awo wa libalatsa tsawamanya ka Petiri na Yohane tsawakala iwanu mbughilambughila ing'awasomile bae, apfo wakangawala kuwona pfawalongile pfinoghile, wamanya kuwa wahamwe na Yesu. 14 Lekeni kwaapfila wamwona imunu yahonetsighwe kema hamwe na Petiri na Yohane, ng'awadahile bae kulonga ichinu chochose. 15 Apfo wawalaghitsa walawe kunze kwe libalatsa, kuya wandusa kwilongetsa iwenyegho. 16 Weghutsa, “Tuwatende choni iwanu wano? Chila imunu iyokala Yerusalemu komanya kuwa watenda chihulo chikulu, na twetwe ng'atudaha bae kubela. 17 Lekeni ili imbuli ino ileke kwenela ng'ani kwe iwanu, tuwakanye waleke kulonga keli ne imunu wowose kwa taghwa lya Yesu.”
 	 18 Kuya wawakema keli mng'anda, wawalaghitsa waleke kulonga keli na kulangulitsa kwa taghwa lya Yesu. 19 Lekeni Petiri na Yohane wawedika, “Mlamle mwemwe muwenyegho, chihi ichinoghile kwe Imulungu, kuwahulikitsa mwemwe au kumuhulikitsa Imulungu. 20 Kwaapfila ng'atudaha bae kuleka kulonga aghala ghatwonile na ghatuhulike.” 21 Kuya iwabala awo wa libaratsa wawakanya ghendo na kuwalekelela. Ng'awadahile bae kuweng'a atsabu kwaapfila iwanu wose wakala womtunitsa Imulungu kwa achila ichilawile. 22 Imunu ayo iyahonetsighwe tsakakala imbala wa kubita miyaka alubaini.
 	
 Iwamtoghole Yesu wolomba wongetsighwe ingupfu

 	23 Bahala Petiri na Yohane hawalekilighwe, woya kwa weyawo, wawalongela achila chawalongelighwe ne iwatambika wakulu ne iwabala. 24 Nawo hawahulike imbuli ayo wamlomba Imulungu kwa ghumoyo ghumwe. “Imtwatsa, ghweghwe kwa Maumba yulumbile kulanga na iisi, ne ibahali na pfose ipfili mumo! 25 Tsakulonga kwa Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka kubitila kwa imtumighwa wako, aba wetu Daudi,
 	‘Ebali wanu wali muisi waghudubuka?
 	Mbona iwanu wokwalangula ipfinu ipfilihela mana?
 	 26 Iwandewa we iisi weyandaa,
 	ne iwatawala watingana hamwe,
 	kumpinga Imtwatsa na Kiristu wake.’
 	 27 Kwaapfila Herodi, Pontiyo Pilato, iwanu we Isiraeli ne iwanu iwali si Wayahudi watingana mne ghumji ghuno kumpinga Yesu, Imtumighwa wako Mwenzeluka, yumsaghule yawe Kiristu. 28 Tsawatingana watenda aghala ghubamile kulawa ghumwande kwa uwetso wako ghalawile. 29 Lelo ghwe Imtwatsa, ulole pfawatutenda tupfuke, utwapfile twetwe iwatumwa wako tudahe kulonga imbuli yako bila kupfuka. 30 Gholosa ghumoko ghwako kuhonetsa iwanu, utende ipfitango na pfihulo kwa taghwa lya Yesu Imtumighwa wako Mwenzeluka.”
 	 31 Hawamalitse kulomba, hanu hala hawatinganile tsahahighisighwa. Wose wamemesighwa Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka, na waghendelela kulonga imbuli ye Imulungu bila kupfuka.
 	
 Iwamtoghole Yesu tsawakala ka iwanu wa lukolo lumwe

 	32 Iwanu wose iwatoghole tsawakala na ghumoyo ghumwe na tsawalangula chinu chimwe. Kuduhu imunu wowose iyalongile ka ichinu iyalinacho chake aliyeka, ila wegholela ipfinu pfose pfawakalile napfo. 33 Iwatumighwa waghendelela kulonga kwa ngupfu Imbuli ya ukutsilihuka kwa Yesu, na Imulungu kawabaliki ghendo. 34 Tsahaduhu imunu wowose iyakalile kahela ichinu. Iwanu iwakalile ne imighunda au tsing'anda tsawang'ali wohutsa, na waghala sendi 35 kwe iwatumighwa, nawo tsawatsighola kwa chila imunu ka pfayabamile.
 	 36 Tsakukala na Mlawi yumwe iyolawila Kupulo, iyakemighwe Yosefu. Iwatumighwa tsawamwing'a taghwa Balinaba, mana yake “Mghuma ghumoyo iwanu” 37 Ayu tsakakala na mghunda, kauhutsa, kasola sendi atso katsighala kwe iwatumighwa.
 
 Ghamatendo 5

 Ananiya na Safila

 	1 Tsakukala ne imunu yumwe iyakemighwe Ananiya na mwehe wake Safila. Nawo pfipfila tsawahutsa mghunda ghwawo. 2 Lekeni Ananiya kabaghula sendi tsingi katsifisa, aku mwehe wake kapfimanya. Sendi itsisighale katsighala kwe iwatumighwa. 3 Petiri kamghutsa, “Ananiya, ebali kumleka Setani yengile mmoyo mwako, na kukutenda umghutsukile Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka, kwa kupfisa sendi tsingi tsupatile kwa kuhutsa mghunda? 4 Pfii mghunda ng'aghukalile ghwako bae hala ng'ana ghuhutsighwe? Na hauutsile sendi atso ambe tsikala tsako, utsitendele chochose choubama. Ebali lelo kulamla kutenda ichinu chino? Ng'umghutsukile imunu bae, ila kumghutsukila Imulungu!” 5 Bahala Ananiya hayahulike apfo, kaghwa hasi, kafa. Iwanu wose iwahulike imbuli ayo wapfuka ng'ani. 6 Kuya iwasongolo watsa, walupfatsa sanda lukuli lwake, wamlapfa kunze, wamtsika.
 	 7 Masaa madatu haghabitile, mwehe wake naye kengila, ng'amanyile bae aghala ighalawile. 8 Petiri kamghutsa, “Unongele, atsino tsitso sendi tsose tsampatile ghweghwe na mmale wako kwa kuhutsa mghunda ghwenu?”
 	Naye kedika, “Ona, tsitso.”
 	 9 Petiri kamlongela, “Ebali ghweghwe na mmale wako mlamula kumghetsa Ghumuhe Mwenzeluka ghwe Imtwatsa? Tegheletsa, iwanu iwamtsikile mmale wako, sambi wa hane libani, nawo pfipfila watsokusola ghweghwe!” 10 Bahala ipinga ayo kaghwa mmaghulu mwa Petiri, kafa. Kuya iwasongolo wala wengila, wampfika ma kafa. Apfo wamlapfa naye kunze, wamtsika habehi na mmale wake. 11 Iwanu wose iwamtoghole Yesu ne iwanu wangi iwahulike mbuli atso wapfuka ng'ani.
 	
 Iwatumighwa wowahonetsa iwanu wengi

 	12 Iwatumighwa tsawatenda pfihulo na pfinu pfingi pfa kukangawatsa mghati mwe iwanu. Na iwanu wose iwatoghole wang'ali wotingana hamwe mne chitala cha mtingano cha Selemani. 13 Kuduhu imunu wowose ing'ayamtoghole Yesu iyaghetsile kwilunga nawo. Hata apfo, iwanu wangi tsawang'ali wowatunya. 14 Iwanu iwamtoghole Imtwatsa wang'ali wakongetseka ng'ani, iwamale ne iwapinga. 15 Mbaka iwanu wang'ali wowaghala iwatamu mne tsinzila na kuwawasisa mlutsatsi na mne ghamatemvu ili Petiri ang'abita sisila lyake liwabitile wangi wawo. 16 Iwanu wengi, iwalawile mne miwambo ya habehi na Yerusalemu watsa, wawaghala iwatamu na iwanu wane ipfinyamkela, nawo wose wahonetsighwa.
 	
 Iwatumighwa wodununzighwa

 	17 Kuya Imtambika mkulu na weyaghe, iwanu we chikingili cha Masadukayo wa hanu hala, wawonela chepfu iwatumighwa. 18 Wawaghogha Iwatumighwa, wawoha mwigheletsa. 19 Lekeni nechilo malaika we Imtwatsa kapfughula imibani ya ligheletsa, kawalapfa kunze, kawalongela, 20 “Mghende, mkeme mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu, muwalongele iwanu imbuli yose ye ughima uno wa sambi.” 21 Iwatumighwa wahulikitsa, kuya nemitondotondo wengila mne Ing'anda ye Imulungu, wandusa kulangulitsa.
 	Imtambika mkulu na weyaghe hawapfikile, wawakema hamwe iwanu we libaratsa kulu lye iwabala we Isiraeli, kuya wawatuma iwanu mchifungo wawaghalile iwatumighwa wala. 22 lekeni iwanu wala hawapfikile ako, ng'awawapfikile bae iwatumighwa wa Yesu mwigheletsa. Apfo woya mne libaratsa na kuwalongela imbuli ayo, 23 walonga, “Tupfika ligheletsa lihindighwa pfipfila, na iwakalitsi wokalitsa imibani.
